HarbourBuilder - Cross-platform visual IDE for Harbour
=======================================================

2026-05-11

  - fix(win): the in-IDE code editor could fail with "Cannot load
    Scintilla.dll / Lexilla.dll" when the IDE exe and the bundled
    Scintilla/Lexilla DLLs had different bitness (e.g. a 32-bit
    hbbuilder_win.exe next to 64-bit DLLs — LoadLibrary returns NULL
    on an arch mismatch). resources/ now has x86/ and x64/ subdirs,
    each holding the matching Scintilla.dll + Lexilla.dll; InitScintilla
    picks the subdir from sizeof(void*) (falls back to the legacy flat
    resources/ then the exe dir then cwd). build_win.bat Step 4 copies
    the DLL set matching the built exe's architecture. Added
    build_scintilla_x86.bat to (re)build the 32-bit DLLs from
    resources/scintilla_src via MSVC x86.

  - fix(win): IDE startup took ~45 seconds. CreatePalette() applies a
    per-component PNG icon (~130 of them) via UI_PaletteSetCompIcon,
    and TComponentPalette::SetCompIcon called ShowTab() on every one —
    that destroys and recreates all palette button windows AND creates
    a fresh tooltip window per button without ever destroying the old
    ones, so ~130 iterations leaked thousands of USER windows and the
    cost ballooned non-linearly. SetCompIcon now just stores the bitmap
    and does one coalesced RedrawWindow(RDW_INVALIDATE|RDW_ALLCHILDREN)
    — WM_DRAWITEM already reads FCompIconOverride[]. Also: LoadPng32 /
    LoadPngSized no longer GdiplusStartup+GdiplusShutdown on every image
    (a process-lifetime GDI+ token is initialised once). Startup time
    went from ~46 s to ~1.4 s.

  - fix(win): the IDE exe had no application manifest, so the process
    started DPI-unaware (the Harbour GT layer creates its window before
    Main() runs SetDPIAware()) and Windows bitmap-stretched the first
    paint — blurry/"deformed" title, menu and toolbars for the first
    seconds. Added source/hbbuilder_win.rc which embeds
    resources/app.manifest (dpiAware + Common-Controls v6); build_win.bat
    gained a "Step 2b" that compiles it with rc.exe (MSVC) / brcc32
    (BCC) / windres (MinGW) and links the resource.

  - tweak(win): main IDE bar (oIDE) is 60 px shorter on screens
    >= 1920 px wide (nBarH -= 60 when nUIScale >= 1.0). Added startup
    timing instrumentation (StTime() -> c:\HarbourBuilder\startup_timing.log)
    covering each Main() phase and the sub-steps of CreatePalette().

  - fix(win): in-IDE "Build Project" now uses the MSVC toolset whose
    architecture matches the installed Harbour libs. The compiler scan
    and all three build paths (TBBuild, DebugApp build, bundled-Harbour
    build batch in EnsureHarbour) were hardcoded to the 32-bit toolset
    (bin\Hostx86\x86\cl.exe / link.exe, lib\x86) — linking against an
    x64 Harbour produced LNK4272 "machine type 'x64' conflicts with
    'x86'" plus ~150 unresolved _HB_FUN_* / _hb_* externals and
    _WinMain@16. ScanCompilers now probes both Hostx64\x64\cl.exe and
    Hostx86\x86\cl.exe per MSVC version and registers a separate entry
    for each (labelled "... x64" / "... x86", x64 listed first as the
    auto-default). The registry array gained a 6th element, cArch
    ("x64" | "x86"); the build paths derive \bin\Host<arch>\<arch>,
    \lib\<arch>, ucrt\<arch>, um\<arch> and a /MACHINE: link flag from
    it. BCC / MinGW entries are tagged with their arch too.

  - fix(win-ai): AI Assistant no longer pops a modal MessageBox on
    panel open when no backend (Ollama / DeepSeek key) is available —
    it just writes a one-line hint to the chat log. The install prompt
    is shown only when the user actually sends a prompt to a local
    (Ollama) model and Ollama isn't found (s_aiOnSend).

  - tweak(win): main IDE bar (oIDE) is 5 px shorter (nBarH -= 5).

2026-05-03b

  - fix(win-ai): runtime dark-mode toggle now propagates to the AI
    panel. The panel was created once with hardcoded #1E1E1E chat +
    #2D2D30 panel bg — WM_CTLCOLOREDIT/STATIC always returned dark
    regardless of g_bDarkIDE, and ToggleDarkMode never told the panel
    to repaint. Fixes:
      - WM_CTLCOLOREDIT / WM_CTLCOLORSTATIC for chat + input now branch
        on g_bDarkIDE (white bg + dark text in light mode).
      - WM_ERASEBKGND always FillRect — dark brush in dark mode,
        COLOR_BTNFACE in light — so a former dark fill doesn't survive
        when wc.hbrBackground was NULL.
      - New HB_FUNC( W32_AIRefreshTheme ): re-applies
        DwmSetWindowAttribute, drops cached panel + chat brushes,
        invalidates panel + chat + input + chips bar, and
        SetWindowPos(SWP_FRAMECHANGED) so DWM re-frames the title bar.
      - ToggleDarkMode calls W32_AIRefreshTheme alongside the existing
        IDE / inspector / design-form / code-editor refresh hooks.

  - fix(win-ai): AI-built controls now materialize on the design form.
    AIBuildForm called UI_*New which only added the C++ control to the
    form's children list — the HWND was never created because
    TForm::Show had already run. Code tab got the new METHODs but
    buttons/edits/etc. stayed invisible. Fix: call
    UI_FormCreateChildren( hForm ) at the end of AIBuildForm so each
    child's CreateHandle runs. Same idea as the macOS/Linux
    UI_FormRealizeChildren we previously stripped.

  - fix(win-ai): full UTF-8 round-trip for accented characters.
    LLM returns UTF-8; Win32 EDIT created via CreateWindowExA stored
    bytes as ANSI codepage so "á" (0xC3 0xA1) rendered as "Ã¡" in chat.
    Switched the chat output and input fields to CreateWindowExW (true
    Unicode windows). s_aiAppend now MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8) +
    SendMessageW(EM_REPLACESEL). s_aiOnSend reads input via
    GetWindowTextW + WideCharToMultiByte(CP_UTF8). Chip click writes
    via SetWindowTextW. s_aiSetChips creates BUTTONs via
    CreateWindowExW with wide labels.

  - feat(win-ai): when AIDispatchReply hits the "[Empty response]" path
    the chat now also dumps the first 500 chars of the raw HTTP body —
    makes it possible to tell at a glance whether curl returned
    nothing, an HTML error page, or a JSON shape we don't recognise.

  - feat(win-ai): UI tweaks across several iterations —
      - Panel auto-opens at IDE startup; WS_EX_TOPMOST so it floats
        above the main IDE window.
      - Anchored to the right edge of the screen workarea, vertically
        centered (SystemParametersInfo SPI_GETWORKAREA), matching the
        macOS NSScreen.visibleFrame / Linux gdk_monitor_get_workarea
        behaviour.
      - Default size 490x820 (was 420x560); initial layout now driven
        from GetClientRect via s_aiRelayout so children honour the
        title bar + frame inset and survive a user drag-resize.
      - Full dark-mode coverage when g_bDarkIDE: panel bg via
        WM_ERASEBKGND (#2D2D30), input EDIT joins chat in
        WM_CTLCOLOREDIT dark scheme (#1E1E1E), labels/status/chips bar
        repaint with panel bg in WM_CTLCOLORSTATIC.
      - Bigger fonts: UI Segoe UI 11pt (was DEFAULT_GUI_FONT ~8pt),
        chat Consolas 12pt (was 10pt). Layout heights bumped to fit.
      - DeepSeek items always at the top of the model combo (default
        deepseek-v4-flash), matching the Linux behaviour. The /key
        sk-... command unlocks the backend; until then selecting a
        deepseek-* model just shows the "key not set" hint.
      - Model combo width reserves room for the Clear button (combo
        was overshooting Clear by ~50 px at the default panel size).

2026-05-03

  - feat(win-ai): full Win32 port of the AI Assistant, matching the
    macOS and GTK3 implementations. New HbAIPanel registered window
    class with AIPanelWndProc dispatching WM_COMMAND (Send/Clear),
    WM_AI_REPLY (worker -> UI marshaling via PostMessage),
    WM_AI_APPEND, WM_AI_SETCHIPS, WM_CTLCOLOREDIT/STATIC/ERASEBKGND
    for full dark-mode coverage (#1E1E1E chat + input, #2D2D30 panel
    bg), and WM_SIZE -> s_aiRelayout for resize. Auto-opens at IDE
    startup, anchored right side of screen workarea + vertically
    centered, WS_EX_TOPMOST so it floats above the main IDE.
    UI font Segoe UI 11pt, chat font Consolas 12pt. Default 490x820
    panel; Send button + Clear; Enter-key submit via input EDIT
    subclass; suggestion chips bar that destroys + recreates BUTTON
    children sized to text via subclassed STATIC parent.

  - feat(win-ai-backend): curl.exe-driven HTTP layer (ships with
    Win10 1803+ — no libcurl dep, no DLL bloat). ai_send_thread
    worker thread builds JSON payload to %TEMP%\hbb_ai_req_<pid>.json,
    runs curl -d @file with stdout pipe, ReadFile loop with 1 MB cap,
    posts WM_AI_REPLY back to UI thread. Ollama probe via
    s_aiFetchOllamaTags (curl /api/tags), s_aiOllamaInstalled
    (where ollama), s_aiTryStartOllama (ShellExecute + 3-sec poll).
    If Ollama installed but no models: background `ollama pull
    gemma3`. If neither Ollama nor DeepSeek key: MessageBox install
    prompt opens https://ollama.com/download. DeepSeek key
    persistence at %USERPROFILE%\.hbbuilder_deepseek_key (or
    DEEPSEEK_API_KEY env). `/key sk-...` saves inline.

  - feat(win-ai-skill): same FORM / CODE / RUN / ADD_CODE / CHAT
    skill as macOS/Linux, embedded as AI_SYS_PROMPT C string literal
    (verbatim port of cocoa_editor.mm:3078-3308 with
    Cocoa->Win32 palette tab naming). JSON parsing on PRG side via
    hb_jsonDecode + balanced-brace recovery in AIDispatchReply,
    dispatching by shape to AIBuildForm / AIAddCode / AIRunProject /
    chat. AIDescribeActiveForm + AIDescribeDbf inject context so the
    LLM sees existing controls and real DBF schemas. AIBuildForm
    upserts controls by name (move/resize/relabel without dupes).
    Stripped 3 case branches Win32 lacks (TStaticText, TScrollBox,
    TLabeledEdit) + UI_FormRealizeChildren (Cocoa-only). 21 control
    types reachable.

  - feat(win-codeeditor): four CodeEditor HB_FUNC wrappers added to
    bring Win32 in line with macOS/Linux backends —
    CodeEditorGetActiveTab (1-based), CodeEditorGetText2 (per-tab,
    falls back to live Scintilla SCI_GETTEXT for active tab),
    CodeEditorMarkLines (Scintilla SCI_MARKERDEFINE +
    SC_MARK_BACKGROUND, marker 5 reserved for AI), CodeEditorClearMarks.
    Required by AIAddCode to highlight the inserted code with an
    olive background.

  - chore(win-build): drop legacy bcc32 source/build_now.bat and
    source/link_now.bat. The canonical build entry is build_win.bat
    at repo root which auto-detects MSVC x86/x64, BCC, MinGW.
    bcc32 path produced 32-bit binaries incompatible with the
    project's 64-bit Scintilla/Lexilla DLLs.

  - fix(win-inspector): hoist `int dampedDpi` declaration to top of
    block in INS_CREATE — bcc32 strict C89 rejected
    decl-after-statement (E2140).

2026-05-02e

  - feat(linux-designform): default form geometry tuned to
    Left=823, Top=392, Width=562, Height=315 so Form1 lands
    consistently inside the editor area on 1920x1080 displays.

  - feat(linux-ai-default-model): AI Assistant panel now lists
    deepseek-v4-flash + deepseek-chat unconditionally at the top
    of the model combo, with deepseek-v4-flash selected by default.
    Ollama models still appear after them when the daemon is up.
    `/key sk-...` saves the DeepSeek API key without re-shuffling
    the combo (entries are already there).

  - feat(linux-ai): port the macOS AI Assistant rework to GTK3.
    hbbuilder_linux.prg gains AIRunProject / AIResizeForm / AIFitForm /
    AIDescribeDbf / AIDescribeActiveForm / AIGetActiveFormClass /
    AIAddCode / AIBuildForm plus AI_FindCtrlByName +
    AI_RewriteClassName helpers — same shape as the Cocoa port so
    the same skill prompt routes through hb_dynsymFindName +
    hb_vmFunction. AIBuildForm uses upsert-by-name, accepts
    items/text/x/y/w/h/title/code, and dispatches to all 24 control
    types reachable from the macOS palette.

  - feat(linux-ai-controls): four new HB_FUNCs in gtk3_core.c —
    UI_StaticTextNew / UI_ScrollBoxNew / UI_LabeledEditNew /
    UI_ProgressBarNew — using existing CT_STATICTEXT / CT_SCROLLBOX /
    CT_LABELEDEDIT / CT_PROGRESSBAR widget paths. Plus
    UI_FormRealizeChildren( hForm ) so AI-driven runtime additions
    materialize their GtkWidgets when the form was already shown.
    Plus CodeEditorMarkLines / CodeEditorClearMarks (Scintilla
    SCI_MARKERDEFINE + SC_MARK_BACKGROUND, marker 5) so AIAddCode
    can highlight the inserted lines with an olive background.

  - feat(linux-ai-panel): GTK AI Assistant panel rebuilt around the
    same FORM / CODE / RUN / ADD_CODE / CHAT skill as macOS.
    Singleton GtkWindow auto-opens at IDE startup, anchored right
    side of the primary monitor and vertically centered (450x600).
    Top bar: model combo populated from /api/tags (curl) plus
    deepseek-v4-flash + deepseek-chat when a key is configured;
    GtkSpinner + Clear button. Suggestion-chip row above the input
    refreshes per turn from the model's "next":[...] field, with
    context-aware defaults (form-mod vs form-create) when the model
    omits it. Click a chip → fills + sends.

  - feat(linux-ai-deepseek): DeepSeek backend alongside Ollama.
    Reads DEEPSEEK_API_KEY env var or ~/.hbbuilder_deepseek_key.
    Inline `/key sk-...` saves the key and unlocks the deepseek
    models (combo prepends them, default selection switches). Routing
    by selected model: deepseek* → POST api.deepseek.com (OpenAI
    shape, Bearer auth); otherwise Ollama localhost:11434/api/chat.
    Response parser handles Ollama (`message.content`), OpenAI
    (`choices[0].message.content`) and `error.message` shapes, with
    balanced-brace recovery for malformed JSON.

  - feat(linux-ai-context): every send prepends ACTIVE FORM
    (AIDescribeActiveForm) and DBF FIELDS (AIDescribeDbf when the
    prompt mentions a *.dbf path) so the LLM operates on the real
    designer state and uses real field names. Dispatch:
    {"action":"run"} → AIRunProject; {"action":"add_code","code":"…"}
    → AIAddCode + olive line markers; controls/w/h/title → AIBuildForm
    (followed by AIAddCode if "code" is present); text → chat reply.
    LLM call runs through a self-contained Python helper written to
    ${TMPDIR}/hbbuilder_ai_helper.py at panel-open time; payload
    transported via base64-encoded env vars (AI_SYS_B64 / AI_USR_B64).

2026-05-02d

  - feat(macos-ai-additional): Additional-palette controls reachable
    from AIBuildForm. Three new HB_FUNCs in cocoa_core.m:
    UI_StaticTextNew, UI_ScrollBoxNew, UI_LabeledEditNew. Existing
    UI_SpeedBtnNew / UI_MaskEditNew / UI_StringGridNew / UI_BitBtnNew /
    UI_ImageNew / UI_ShapeNew / UI_BevelNew now wired through AIBuildForm.
    Allowed control-type whitelist expanded accordingly. Skill carries
    the actual HbBuilder palette catalog (Standard / Additional /
    Cocoa) so the model stops describing Delphi-only controls
    (TTrayIcon, TMediaPlayer, TChart, …) when asked to list components.

  - feat(macos-ai-suggestions): Skill drives the chip suggestions —
    every JSON response MUST include "next":[3-4 short prompts].
    AIBuildForm/AIAddCode/RUN responses include them; CHAT and CODE
    responses are now also JSON-wrapped: {"text":"...","next":[...]}.
    Obj-C parses "next" from the response; falls back to context-aware
    defaults (form-mod chips when an active form exists, form-create
    chips otherwise) only if the model omits it. Chip row implemented
    as NSStackView above the input; chips refresh after each turn,
    click → fills input + sends.

  - feat(macos-ai-upsert): AIBuildForm consolidated into a single path
    that upserts controls by name. New AI_FindCtrlByName helper looks
    up an existing child by its cName; if found, AIBuildForm UPDATES
    its props (nLeft/nTop/nWidth/nHeight/cText/aItems) instead of
    creating a duplicate. Lets the model emit "centra los botones",
    "muévelo abajo", etc. by re-emitting controls with the same name
    and new x/y. Skill carries explicit examples and a rule: never
    refuse a move/center request.

  - feat(macos-ai-items): Control spec accepts "items":[...] for
    TTreeView / TListBox / TComboBox / TListView. AIBuildForm calls
    UI_SetProp(hCtrl, "aItems", items) which goes through FHeaders +
    reload-data, so items appear in the design preview AND at runtime.
    Skill instructs the model to populate via "items" inline rather
    than emitting a Form1Show populator.

  - feat(macos-ai-context): Active-form context fed to LLM on every
    send. AIDescribeActiveForm() returns JSON of class, title, size
    and existing controls. Obj-C prepends it to the user message.
    Skill rule: emitting a control with an existing name UPDATES that
    control; behavior wiring goes via ADD_CODE on existing controls.
    AIGetActiveFormClass() also feeds the actual TFormN class name so
    generated METHODs target the right class. AI_RewriteClassName is
    a defensive backstop that rewrites stale "CLASS T<name>" the model
    emits to the real active class.

  - feat(macos-ai-deepseek): DeepSeek backend support alongside Ollama.
    Reads DEEPSEEK_API_KEY env or ~/.hbbuilder_deepseek_key; inline
    "/key sk-..." stores and unlocks. When DeepSeek is configured the
    Ollama probe + banner is skipped; combo gets deepseek-v4-flash +
    deepseek-chat at the top. Routing by selected model: deepseek* →
    POST https://api.deepseek.com/v1/chat/completions with Bearer auth
    and OpenAI-shape payload. Response parser handles Ollama shape,
    OpenAI shape, and {"error":{"message":...}}.

  - fix(macos-tbrun-cache): FNV-1a 32-bit hash over the FULL project
    code, replacing the previous 5000-byte position-weighted sum that
    let small AI-driven edits (centering a button, renaming text) slip
    through unchanged so the cached app launched instead of being
    rebuilt. Also fixes "run sometimes executes the previous project."

  - fix(macos-ai-blockscope): Hoist `id specObj` out of the inner
    dispatch_async-main block (declared `__block id specObj = nil`
    inside the URL completion handler) so the second main-queue block
    that drives suggestion-chip refresh can read the parsed JSON. Was
    a build-breaking compile error; once fixed, model-supplied "next"
    chips actually populate.

  - feat(macos-ai-events): AIAddCode triggers SyncDesignerToCode after
    appending so Form-event-handler methods auto-wire by name (e.g.
    METHOD Form1Click → ::OnClick := { || ::Form1Click() } emitted in
    CreateForm). Skill documents the naming convention: control event
    handler = controlName + event-without-On (btnOkClick); form event
    handler = formName + event-without-On (Form1Click).

  - feat(macos-ai-types): Allowed types include TTreeView, TListView,
    TListBox, TProgressBar, TImage, TBevel, TShape, TBitBtn,
    TTabControl, TMaskEdit, TStringGrid, TSpeedButton, TStaticText,
    TScrollBox, TLabeledEdit. Each dispatches to its UI_*New entry
    point. TMaskEdit's "text" field carries the input mask
    (e.g. "99/99/9999").

  - feat(macos-ai-panel): AI Assistant panel polish.
    * Title simplified to "AI Assistant" (no "(Ollama)" suffix).
    * Default width 420 → 450 px.
    * Suggestion chips row above the input; chat scroll moves up to
      make room.
    * Banner conditional on backend: "(DeepSeek)" when configured,
      Ollama wording otherwise.

2026-05-02c

  - feat(macos-ai-deepseek): DeepSeek backend alongside Ollama. Reads
    DEEPSEEK_API_KEY env var or ~/.hbbuilder_deepseek_key. Inline
    command "/key sk-..." stores the key and unlocks the model. The
    model combo gets "deepseek-v4-flash" + "deepseek-chat" when a key
    is present. Routing decided by selected model name: deepseek* →
    POST https://api.deepseek.com/v1/chat/completions with Bearer auth
    and OpenAI-shape payload; otherwise → Ollama as before. Response
    parser handles both shapes (Ollama {"message":{"content":...}} and
    OpenAI {"choices":[{"message":{"content":...}}]}) plus error shape
    {"error":{"message":...}}. When DeepSeek is configured the Ollama
    probe + banner is skipped — title shows "AI Assistant" only.

  - feat(macos-ai-ctx): Active-form context fed to LLM on every send.
    * AIDescribeActiveForm() returns JSON of active form (class, title,
      size, controls with name/type/text/bounds). Obj-C prepends
      "ACTIVE FORM (currently open in the designer): {...}" to the
      user message.
    * Skill rule: emitting a control whose name already exists UPDATES
      that control (move/center/resize/relabel). Emit ADD_CODE for
      handlers on existing controls. Only emit new "controls" entries
      for genuinely new controls. Skill explicitly forbids refusing
      move/center requests with concrete few-shot examples.

  - feat(macos-ai-formspec): AIBuildForm consolidated into a single
    path — no resize/fit/add-current branches. Rule: "title" key
    signals NEW form (MenuNewForm); otherwise the active form is the
    target. Form-level title/w/h applied when present. Each control
    in "controls" is upserted by name via new AI_FindCtrlByName helper:
    if a child with the same cName exists, props are updated in place;
    otherwise a new control is created.

  - feat(macos-ai-types): Allowed control types expanded to TTreeView,
    TListView, TListBox, TProgressBar, TImage, TBevel, TShape, TBitBtn,
    TTabControl. Each dispatches to the corresponding UI_*New entry
    point.

  - feat(macos-ai-items): Control spec accepts an "items":[...] array
    for TTreeView/TListBox/TComboBox/TListView. AIBuildForm calls
    UI_SetProp(hCtrl, "aItems", items) which pipes through to FHeaders
    + reload-data, so items appear in the design preview AND at
    runtime. Skill instructs the model to use "items" inline rather
    than emitting a Form1Show populator.

  - feat(macos-ai-dbf-context): Regex-detect ".dbf" in user message,
    call AIDescribeDbf(cPath) which dbUseArea + dbStruct, prepend the
    JSON field list to the user message so the model uses real names.
    Few-shot example for orders.dbf shows correct Harbour syntax
    (orders->FIELD, dbSkip/dbCommit, ::oedtX:cText).

  - feat(macos-ai-class-rewrite): Active-form class context fed to LLM
    so generated METHODs target the right TFormN class. Defensive
    backstop: AI_RewriteClassName scans the generated code for
    "CLASS T<identifier>" patterns and rewrites each to the actual
    active class (manual char-loop — hb_regexReplace is not linked).
    AIAddCode triggers SyncDesignerToCode after appending so events
    auto-wire by name (Form1Click, btnOkClick, ::OnClick := { || ::X() }).

  - feat(macos-ai-suggestions): NSStackView suggestion-chip row above
    the input. Chips populated at startup with starter prompts
    ("haz un login", "añade ok y cancel", "ajusta tamaño form", "run")
    and refreshed after each turn — when an active form exists, chips
    show form-mod prompts; otherwise form-creation prompts. Click a
    chip → fills the input and sends.

  - feat(macos-ai-panel): Panel +30px wider (420 → 450). Title
    simplified to "AI Assistant" (no "(Ollama)" suffix). Bottom row
    layout adjusted: input shrinks 20px to make room for spinner;
    chat scroll moves up 34px to make room for the suggestion row.

2026-05-02b

  - feat(macos-ai-skill): AI Assistant skill expanded — single LLM
    dispatch path now covers FORM (new), FORM (current), RUN, ADD_CODE,
    CODE, CHAT.
    * No regex intent detection — LLM classifies. Detection is
      shape-based: response with "controls" key + title/w/h → new form;
      "controls" alone (no title) → add to current form; {"action":"run"}
      → AIRunProject (TBRun); {"action":"add_code","code":"..."} →
      AIAddCode appends to active editor tab; plain text → chat.
    * Form spec can include optional "code" field with event-handler
      methods. After AIBuildForm runs, the code is appended via
      AIAddCode. SyncDesignerToCode then auto-wires events by name
      (METHOD btnOkClick → ::OnClick := { || ::btnOkClick() }).
    * Method-naming convention documented in the skill: control
      handlers = controlName + event-without-On (btnOkClick,
      cboColorChange); form handlers = formName + event-without-On
      (Form1Click, Form2Show). Few-shot examples updated.

  - feat(macos-ai-dbf): DBF data-entry-form generation.
    * New public Harbour function AIDescribeDbf( cPath ) opens the DBF
      via dbUseArea, captures dbStruct, returns a JSON array of
      {name,type,len,dec}. Resolves cPath as-is, then relative to
      project base, then to cwd.
    * Obj-C side regex-detects ".dbf" in the user message, calls
      AIDescribeDbf, and prepends "DBF FIELDS (real schema of ...): [...]"
      to the user message before sending to Ollama. The skill instructs
      the model to use those exact field names, build TLabel + TEdit
      rows + nav row (btnFirst/Prev/Next/Last/Save), and emit
      USE/dbSkip/dbCommit-style Harbour code.
    * Few-shot example for orders.dbf demonstrates correct Harbour:
      `orders->FIELD` access, `::oedtX:cText` for control text,
      Form1Show + Refresh helper + nav/save methods.

  - feat(macos-ai-run): {"action":"run"} dispatches to new public
    Harbour function AIRunProject which calls TBRun() (build + launch).

  - feat(macos-ai-codehighlight): new HB_FUNCs CodeEditorMarkLines and
    CodeEditorClearMarks use Scintilla SCI_MARKERDEFINE +
    SC_MARK_BACKGROUND + alpha 90 to highlight AI-inserted line ranges.
    Color olive (0x008080 BGR). AIAddCode clears prior marks then
    highlights from the first new line to the last.

  - fix(macos-ai-json): balanced-brace JSON recovery. When the primary
    JSON parse fails, scan from the first '{' to its matching '}' (track
    nesting, skip braces inside strings, honour escapes) and parse that
    substring instead. Salvages malformed model output that has trailing
    garbage after the closing brace, e.g. `{...}],"code":"..."}`.

2026-05-02

  - feat(macos-ai): AI Assistant panel reworked end-to-end.
    * Auto-opens at IDE startup, anchored right side of screen and
      vertically centered (right margin 40px).
    * Conversation text rendered in light gray (0.83) via attributed-
      string append helper s_aiAppend(); typingAttributes set so
      programmatically-appended text keeps the color (previous
      mutableString:appendString lost it). Auto-scrolls to bottom on
      every append.
    * Bottom controls (input/Send/Clear) switched from NSViewMinYMargin
      to NSViewMaxYMargin so they stay anchored at the bottom on resize
      instead of drifting up.
    * Pressing Enter in the input field sends the message (target/action
      wired to sendMessage:).
    * Spinning NSProgressIndicator added to the right of the Clear
      button; runs while waiting for Ollama, hidden when idle.
    * On open: detects whether Ollama daemon is running via GET
      localhost:11434/api/tags. If down, tries `open -gja Ollama`,
      falls back to spawning `ollama serve` from /opt/homebrew/bin or
      /usr/local/bin, polls 6s for readiness. If not installed, shows
      NSAlert offering to open https://ollama.com/download.
    * Model combo populated dynamically from /api/tags. If no models
      installed, auto-pulls `gemma3` (latest Gemma in Ollama registry)
      with live progress streamed into the chat.

  - feat(macos-ai-formgen): AI Assistant can now design forms from
    natural-language requests.
    * Single dispatch path: LLM classifies user message into FORM /
      CODE / CHAT and responds in the matching format. FORM responses
      are JSON specs (title/w/h/controls); CODE responses are fenced
      Harbour snippets; CHAT is plain text.
    * Few-shot examples for "dos botones ok y cancel", "haz un login",
      "tres edits"; temperature 0.2 for deterministic layouts.
    * Uses /api/chat with separate system + user roles and strips any
      ```json ... ``` fences the model wraps around the spec.
    * New public Harbour function AIBuildForm( cJson ): decodes via
      hb_jsonDecode, calls MenuNewForm() to spawn a fresh design form,
      applies title/size, drops TLabel/TEdit/TButton/TCheckBox/
      TComboBox/TGroupBox/TRadioButton/TMemo controls via the existing
      UI_*New() entry points, assigns names via UI_SetProp, then runs
      InspectorPopulateCombo + InspectorRefresh + SyncDesignerToCode.
    * Obj-C side calls AIBuildForm via hb_dynsymFindName +
      hb_vmPushDynSym + hb_vmFunction so no Harbour-side polling is
      needed.

  - fix(macos-form-realize): New HB_FUNC UI_FormRealizeChildren( hForm )
    creates NSViews for any HBControl children added after the form is
    already on screen. AIBuildForm calls it after dropping all controls
    so they actually render — previously UI_LabelNew/UI_ButtonNew etc.
    only `addChild`d to the internal array and the views were created
    only at form-show time, leaving programmatically-added controls
    invisible. The helper applies FClientTop offset, re-stacks the
    design overlay on top, and triggers a redraw.

      32-bit exe -> bin\libmysql.dll
      64-bit exe -> bin\libmysql64.dll

    existed for slots 121..130.

    LoadPng32 now produces a 48x48 PARGB bitmap (drawing the
    source PNG up to 40x40, upscaling small 16/24px icons), and
    the owner-draw button caps icon to button area to avoid
    overflow on narrow tabs. Affects every tab including
    Standard.

  - fix(win-toolbar): Toolbar icons no longer render with a
    fuchsia halo around their edges. The DPI-scaling StretchBlt
    used HALFTONE which interpolates pixels, so anti-aliased
    edges blended with the RGB(255,0,255) mask and produced
    near-magenta values that ImageList_AddMasked could not
    strip. Switched to COLORONCOLOR (nearest-neighbor) and
    pre-fill the destination with the mask colour first, so
    edge pixels stay at exact mask RGB and get masked cleanly.

  - feat(win-inspector): Bumped inspector font from 9pt to 13pt
    in source/inspector/inspector_win.prg with combo/tab height
    28 -> 32 to fit. Earlier 9pt variant lived in the regenerated
    hbbuilder_win.c which is overwritten on every Harbour
    compile, so the change had to move into the inspector .prg
    BEGINDUMP block instead.

  - feat(win-ide): Reduced main IDE bar height by 10px
    (nBarH min cap 120 -> 110) so the editor / inspector get a
    bit more vertical real-estate.

2026-04-27a

  - feat(interop): Real implementations for TRust, TNode, TDotNet,
    TJava and TRuby in source/core/classes.prg. All five inherit
    TInteropRuntime and follow the TPython pattern (Start, Stop,
    Exec, Eval, SetVar, GetVar) plus Build/Run for compiled
    runtimes. Auto-detection probes ~/.cargo/bin, /opt/homebrew,
    /usr/local, /usr/bin and PATH; missing toolchains set
    cLastError with the install URL and fire bOnError instead of
    crashing. SetVar values are injected as language-native
    declarations (let/var/=) ahead of the next Eval/Exec so
    Harbour-side state crosses into the foreign runtime without
    extra plumbing. TRust Eval wraps the expression in
    `println!("{:?}", { expr });` (single-quoted string to dodge
    the Harbour preprocessor's `\"` non-escape). TDotNet Build
    synthesizes a one-shot net8.0 csproj with optional
    PackageReference entries (aModules / AddPackage). TJava uses
    a configurable cMainClass and infers the `java` binary from
    cJavacPath. TNode and TRuby write the script to a temp file
    and remove it after run.

  - sample(connectivity): New sample projects for each runtime
    under samples/projects/{rust,node,dotnet,java,ruby}. Layout
    mirrors samples/projects/python: ComboBox samples loader,
    editable script memo, Run / Eval / Build / Clear buttons and
    output log wired to OnReady / OnError / OnOutput / OnBuild.
    TRust sample also exercises SetVar + Eval round-trip so users
    can see Harbour values appearing inside the generated Rust
    main.

  - sample(postgresql): Rebuilt samples/projects/postgresql/
    Form1.prg + Project1.prg to exercise every TPostgreSQL
    surface: cServer / nPort / cUser / cPassword / cDatabase /
    cCharSet plus cTable / cSQL / cIdSequence; bOnConnect /
    bOnDisconnect / bOnError; Open / Close / IsConnected /
    LastError / Tables / TableExists; Execute / direct Query /
    LoadCursor + FieldCount / FieldName / FieldGet / GoTop / Skip
    / Eof for cursor navigation; LastInsertId driven by an
    editable cIdSequence GET. Tables list, SQL editor, cursor
    nav buttons and a per-record memo land on a 820x620 form.

  - docs(connectivity): docs/{en,es,pt}/controls-connectivity.html
    gain a "Runtime Requirements" section after the supported
    languages table. Each row lists the required tool, the macOS
    install command (rustup, brew install node, brew install
    --cask dotnet-sdk, brew install openjdk, brew install ruby,
    brew install go, xcode-select --install, brew install lua)
    and the auto-detect search order. Three follow-up subsections
    document the Execution Model (compile+run vs interpret vs
    embedded, with $TMPDIR artefact paths), Common Events
    (bOnReady/bOnError/bOnOutput/bOnBuild signatures) and the

  - fix(macos-palette): UI_PaletteSetCompIcon overrides now apply to
    components placed past slot 110 of palette.bmp (Connectivity, Git,

2026-04-26k

  - feat(ide-win): Proportional Windows IDE layout. Introduced
    nUIScale (clamped 0.85..1.20 from nScreenW / 1920) and nUIFont
    (Int(11 * nUIScale), min 9pt) statics in hbbuilder_win.prg.
    Bar height, inspector width, designer-form footprint and the
    IDE menu/title font now derive from nUIScale instead of fixed
    pixel constants. CreateDesignForm uses the same proportional
    sizing and clamps X/Y so the designer always fits the work
    area; the previous hardcoded (1129, 456) origin is replaced by
    "centered in editor area, biased 35% from top". Ratios match
    the classic 1024x768 reference (Inspector 24%, Bar 140px) but
    grow/shrink coherently with the screen.

  - feat(toolbar-win): DPI-aware toolbar icon + button scaling.
    TToolBar::LoadImages reads system DPI via GetDeviceCaps and
    rescales the 32x32 source bitmap with HALFTONE StretchBlt
    onto a larger ImageList cell when DPI > 96 (32 -> 48 at 200%,
    button 40 -> 60). A 50% dampening factor keeps icons
    proportional without dominating the bar at high DPI. Falls
    back to the original 32/40 sizes at 96 DPI so legacy displays
    are unchanged.

  - feat(inspector-win): DPI-aware Inspector font + name column.
    INS_CREATE now picks lf.lfHeight from MulDiv( 9, dampedDpi,
    72 ) with the same 50% dampening (96 at 96 DPI, 144 at 192
    DPI), and scales the property/event name column from 205 px
    to MulDiv( 205, dampedDpi, 96 ) (308 px at 200%). COL_NAME_W
    became a runtime variable (s_colNameW) so the rest of the
    inspector keeps reading a single source of truth.

  - feat(win): TPopupMenu — port of the Linux/macOS non-visual
    context-menu component to Win32. Adds UI_PopupMenuNew /
    UI_PopupMenuShow Harbour entry points in hbbridge.cpp.
    BuildPopupHMenu assembles a standalone HMENU on demand from
    the parsed nodes (level 0 = root) and TrackPopupMenu pops it
    at the cursor with the parent form raised to foreground first
    so the keyboard focus dance does not eat the click. Replaced
    the single s_pMenu global with a fixed-size registry
    (s_apMenus[64] + HBW32_IsRegistered/Register) so popups and
    the main menu coexist on the same form. UI_SetProp fast-path
    accepts both kinds and skips BuildHMenu for popups (they are
    rebuilt per show).

  - feat(build-win): MSVC x64 in build_win.bat. vswhere detection
    now offers x86 and x64 as separate compiler choices when both
    cl.exe (Hostx86\x86 + Hostx64\x64) and the matching Harbour
    lib dirs (lib\win\msvc + lib\win\msvc64) are present.
    :build_msvc routes HBLIB / MSVC_BIN / MSVC_LIB / SDK arch
    based on COMPILER_ARCH; UCRT/UM lib paths follow SDK_ARCH.
    Also probes vswhere under both "Program Files" and "Program
    Files (x86)".

  - chore(macos-palette): Removed ReportDesigner (CT 92) from the ERP
    palette tab in hbbuilder_macos.prg — component remained registered
    but was unused / not yet implemented.

  - feat(db-mysql): Real TMySQL implementation via libmysqlclient
    (brew mysql-client 9.6.0). Added source/cocoa_mysql.c exposing
    HBMYSQL_OPEN/CLOSE/EXEC/QUERY/FIELDS/ERROR/LASTID/TABLES bindings
    over the MySQL C API. Replaced the TMySQL stub in source/core/
    classes.prg with a full-featured class:
      * Properties: cServer, nPort, cUser, cPassword, cDatabase,
        cCharSet (sent via SET NAMES, default utf8mb4), lAutoCommit,
        cTable, cSQL (drive cursor navigation).
      * Methods: Open, Close, Execute, Query, Tables, TableExists,
        LastInsertId, LoadCursor, FieldCount/FieldName/GoTop/Eof/
        FieldGet/Skip (DBGrid-compatible cursor).
      * Events: bOnConnect, bOnDisconnect, bOnError (called on Open
        success, Close, and any failure with the libmysqlclient
        message).
    build_mac.sh detects /usr/local/opt/mysql-client and conditionally
    compiles cocoa_mysql.c + links -lmysqlclient.

  - feat(db-mariadb): TMariaDB now fully functional — inherits TMySQL
    so it picks up the libmysqlclient backend transparently. Wire-
    compatible client speaks to both MySQL and MariaDB servers; only
    the cDriver tag differs.

  - feat(db-postgresql): Real TPostgreSQL implementation via libpq
    (brew libpq). Added source/cocoa_pgsql.c with HBPGSQL_OPEN/CLOSE/
    EXEC/QUERY/FIELDS/ERROR/LASTID/TABLES bindings. Replaced the
    TPostgreSQL stub with a full class mirroring TMySQL's API:
    same properties, methods and events plus cIdSequence and an
    optional cSeq parameter on LastInsertId() that maps to PostgreSQL
    CURRVAL semantics. Tables() reads from pg_catalog.pg_tables
    excluding system schemas. build_mac.sh detects /usr/local/opt/
    libpq and conditionally compiles cocoa_pgsql.c + links -lpq.

  - feat(samples): Three new IDE-style sample projects demonstrating
    the database backends end-to-end:
      * samples/projects/mysql      - TMySQL form
      * samples/projects/mariadb    - TMariaDB form
      * samples/projects/postgresql - TPostgreSQL form
    Each project includes Project1.hbp, Project1.prg (wires bOnConnect/
    bOnDisconnect/bOnError + Connect/Execute buttons) and Form1.prg
    (host/port/user/password/database edits, tables listbox, SQL memo,
    output memo, status label).

2026-04-26h

  - fix(linux-popup): TPopupMenu items declared with ACCEL "Ctrl+X"
    were displayed without the accelerator text in the right column of
    the popup. HBPopupMenu_Build was reading every node field except
    n->szShortcut, so the parsed shortcut never reached gtk. Mirror the
    HBMainMenu_Attach logic: parse n->szShortcut with ParseShortcut and
    call gtk_widget_add_accelerator with GTK_ACCEL_VISIBLE on the leaf
    item. Use a private GtkAccelGroup attached to the popup menu (via
    gtk_menu_set_accel_group) instead of the form's s_accelGroup, so
    the labels render but the keys are NOT bound globally — a popup is
    contextual and its shortcuts must not steal focus from edit/memo/
    scintilla widgets on the form. Verified against samples/projects/
    popup which uses Ctrl+X/C/V/A and Ctrl+B/I/U on a sub-popup.

2026-04-26g

  - fix(macos-menu): Keyboard accelerators on NSMenu items rendered as
    blank for any shortcut that wasn't a single character separated by
    "+", e.g. "Ctrl-T" (hyphen), "F1", "Esc", "Up". Replaced the inline
    parser in HBMainMenu_Attach + HBPopupMenu_Build with a single
    HB_ParseShortcut helper that:
      * tokenizes on "+", "-", or whitespace as separators
      * recognizes Ctrl/Control/Cmd/Command, Alt/Opt/Option, Shift,
        Meta/Super as modifier names
      * maps F1..F35 via NSF1FunctionKey
      * maps Esc/Tab/Enter/Return/Space/Backspace, Delete/Del, Home/End,
        PageUp/PageDown, and Up/Down/Left/Right arrows to their
        corresponding Unicode/NSFunctionKey codepoints
      * defaults the modifier mask to Cmd if none parsed
    Both TMainMenu and TPopupMenu items now display their shortcuts
    consistently in the right column of the menu.

  - fix(macos-inspector): The Menu Items Editor's "+Item" / "+SubItem"
    buttons always inserted at level 1 / level 2 — correct for TMainMenu
    (where level 0 is the popup header) but wrong for TPopupMenu (where
    level 0 is the top-level entry). Items added to a TPopupMenu via the
    editor would end up orphaned at level 1 and disappear at runtime
    until the form was saved (codegen + RestoreFromCode collapsed levels
    on round-trip). The editor now queries UI_GetType on entry, and when
    the control is CT_POPUPMENU=201 it shifts "+Item" to level 0,
    "+SubItem" to level 1, and the separator default level accordingly.
    "+Popup" stays at level 0 in both modes.

2026-04-26f

  - feat(macos): TPopupMenu — port of the Linux non-visual context-menu
    component to Cocoa. Palette entry sits next to TMainMenu. Same
    Chr(1)+pipe-serialized aMenuItems as TMainMenu, same MENUITEM/POPUP/
    MENUSEPARATOR DSL with DEFINE POPUPMENU <oPop> / END POPUPMENU
    bookends. CT_POPUPMENU = 201 on macOS (paired with CT_MAINMENU=200);
    classes.prg HB_CreateComponent now accepts both 136 (Linux) and 201
    (Mac). HBPopupMenu_Build assembles a standalone NSMenu on demand and
    pops it via popUpMenuPositioningItem at [NSEvent mouseLocation].
    UI_PopupMenuNew/UI_PopupMenuShow are the Harbour entry points.
    UI_SetProp/GetProp/GetAllProps extended so aMenuItems and aOnClick
    work for both CT_MAINMENU and CT_POPUPMENU. RegenerateFormCode and
    RestoreFormFromCode emit/parse DEFINE POPUPMENU blocks. SF Symbol
    "contextualmenu.and.cursorarrow" for the palette icon on macOS 11+.

  - fix(macos-menu): Captions like "Cu&t" rendered the literal ampersand
    in NSMenu items because Cocoa has no equivalent of Win/GTK mnemonic
    underlines. Added HB_StripMnemonic helper that drops single "&" and
    collapses "&&" to a literal "&". Applied at all three caption sites
    in HBMainMenu_Attach (root popup, sub-popup, leaf item) and the new
    HBPopupMenu_Build, so menu titles display cleanly without the marker
    chars on macOS while staying source-compatible with Win/Linux DSL.

  - fix(macos-form): ::Left/::Top assignments in CreateForm() were lost
    at runtime — the form always centered on screen even when the
    designer had placed it elsewhere. The nLeft/nTop UI_SetProp branches
    only flipped FCenter=NO/FPosition=POS_DESIGNED when FWindow already
    existed, but during CreateForm the NSWindow has not been created yet
    (it is built later by createWindowWithRunLoop). Moved the flag-flip
    out of the FWindow guard so the designed origin survives, and only
    the live setFrameOrigin call stays gated on FWindow != nil.

  - fix(ide-linux): Forms loaded from a project (vs. forms created via
    File > New) did not refresh the code editor or inspector when moved

2026-04-26c

  - fix(gtk3): TMainMenu captions rendered "&File" literally instead of
    showing the F as an Alt-mnemonic. GTK's gtk_menu_item_new_with_mnemonic
    expects "_File" syntax; we were passing the Windows-style "&File"
    captions straight through. Added a hb_amp_to_gtk_mnemonic helper that
    converts "&" -> "_", collapses "&&" to literal "&", and escapes
    existing "_" -> "__" so it renders literally. Applied at the three
    menu builder call sites (root popup, sub-popup, leaf item) and the
    legacy UI_MenuPopupAdd entry point.

  - fix(palette): MainMenu palette button showed the BitBtn "✓Ok" icon
    because palette.bmp was authored when Standard tab had 11 items
    (Label..ScrollBar). Adding TMainMenu as the 12th Standard item
    pushed every Additional-tab icon off by one (BitBtn got the
    SpeedButton lightning, SpeedButton got the Image picture, etc).
    Inserted a synthesized 32×32 menu-bar icon at position 11 in
    resources/palette.bmp (and the macOS bundle copy), shifting icons
    11..108 to 12..109. Realigns MainMenu plus every Additional-tab
    component on Win/Mac/Linux simultaneously.

  - sample(mainmenu): Added the standard keyboard accelerators that the
    Edit and Help popups were missing: Cmd+Z/X/C/V on Undo/Cut/Copy/Paste
    and F1 on About. Without an ACCEL clause MENUITEM does not register
    a shortcut, so the right-aligned hint was blank.

2026-04-26b

  - fix(ide-codegen/linux): TMainMenu generation produced two bugs in
    main.prg. (1) A redundant `::oMenu:aMenuItems := "<serialized>"`
    line was emitted before the DEFINE MENUBAR DSL; when action
    strings contained literal `"` chars (e.g. `EditAction(Self,"Undo")`)
    those quotes broke out of the surrounding string literal, leaking
    `UNDO`/`MENUBAR` as bare tokens — Harbour reported syntax errors
    at lines 48-49. (2) The DSL header was emitted as bare
    `DEFINE MENUBAR` instead of `DEFINE MENUBAR ::oMenuN`, but the
    xcommand `DEFINE MENUBAR <oMenu> => _HBMenuStart(<oMenu>)` requires
    the menu argument. Drop the redundant aMenuItems assignment (the
    DSL already sets it via _HBMenuEnd → TMainMenu_Serialize → ASSIGN
    aMenuItems → UI_SetProp) and add the `::o<ctrl>` argument to the
    DEFINE MENUBAR header, matching the existing macOS/Win32 codegen.

2026-04-26a

  - refactor(menu): TMenuItem now carries its own bAction codeblock —
    aOnClick parallel array is no longer the source of truth. New flow:
    DEFINE MENUBAR DSL captures `{|oMenuItem| <action>}` per MENUITEM
    via the xcommand translator, _HBMenuAdd stores it in TMenuItem:bAction,
    and _HBMenuEnd auto-builds the runtime aOnClick array from items.
    Backends (cocoa/gtk3/win32/hbbridge) untouched — they still receive
    aOnClick via UI_SetProp, just auto-populated instead of user-written.
    IDE codegen on macOS, Linux, Windows drops the redundant
    `::oMenu:aOnClick := { ... }` emission (3 sites — mac CT_MAINMENU=200,
    linux CT_MAINMENU=132, win primary 200 + legacy 132 paths).
    MENUITEM xcommand split into 4 fixed-arg forms (ACTION+ACCEL,
    ACTION-only, ACCEL-only, bare) so the bAction position stays stable.
    Block declares `oMenuItem` param so codegen-emitted
    `ACTION FuncName( Self, oMenuItem )` for bare-name handlers compiles
    cleanly. Sample samples/projects/mainmenu/Form1.prg drops manual
    aOnClick; menu wiring now lives entirely inside DEFINE MENUBAR.

  - fix(ide-parser/mac): RestoreFormFromCode left trailing CR on every
    line when reading CRLF-saved Form1.prg, so exact-match checks
    (`cMLU == "END POPUP"`, `"END MENUBAR"`) silently failed. Result:
    nMenuLevel never decremented between popups, parser produced a
    serial with sibling popups stamped at deeper and deeper levels,
    and codegen-on-Build re-emitted nested `DEFINE POPUP "&Edit"` etc
    inside the previous popup. Now strip Chr(13) before tokenizing,
    matching the linux parser's existing behavior.

  - fix(ide-parser/mac+linux): MENUITEM ACTION parser truncated the
    handler at the first space inside the expression, so
    `FileNew( Self )` became `FileNew(` — codegen then re-emitted
    `ACTION FileNew(` (unbalanced paren, syntax error). Capture the
    full expression up to ` ACCEL "` instead of first whitespace; only
    strip a trailing `()` when the bare name has no other parens.

  - fix(ide-parser/mac+linux): DEFINE MENUBAR detection used exact
    match against "DEFINE MENUBAR" but codegen emits
    `DEFINE MENUBAR ::oMenu1`. Parser silently skipped the block and
    aMenuItems stayed empty after Open. Accept either bare or
    `DEFINE MENUBAR <oMenu>` form (win parser already used a prefix
    match).

2026-04-25e

  - fix(dsl): TMainMenu DEFINE MENUBAR DSL emitted MENUITEM nodes one
    level too deep, so popups appeared on the menubar but their child
    items were never visible at runtime. _HBMenuCtx started nLevel at 1
    and _HBMenuPopup emitted popup at nLevel-1 (=0) then incremented
    nLevel to 2 — subsequent _HBMenuAdd calls stamped MENUITEMs at
    level 2 instead of 1. BuildHMenu (hbbridge.cpp) resolved the parent
    via hStack[nLevel], and hStack[2] was never set for top-level
    popups, so AppendMenuA was called with a NULL HMENU and the items
    silently disappeared.
    Now: nLevel starts at 0, _HBMenuPopup emits at nLevel then ++,
    _HBMenuAdd emits at nLevel, END POPUP decrements. Layout becomes
    popup=0, item=1, sub-popup=1, sub-item=2 — matches the parent
    stack walk in BuildHMenu and the inspector's reverse parser
    (RestoreFormFromCode). Single fix in source/core/classes.prg
    covers Win32, macOS and Linux (shared classes file).

2026-04-25d

  - fix(ide-codegen): TMainMenu codegen produced invalid Harbour when a
    menu handler was a method call like Self:Close. Emit path wrapped
    every cHndl with ( Self, oMenuItem ) and added a stub
    "static function <cHndl>( oForm, oMenuItem )", which yielded
    "static function Self:Close(...)" — Error E0030 syntax error at ':'.
    Codegen now distinguishes expression handlers (contain ':' or '(')
    from bareword identifiers: expressions emit verbatim with a trailing
    "()" appended if missing and no stub is generated; barewords keep
    the auto-wrap + stub behavior. Applied across Win32, macOS, Linux
    backends in both CT_MAINMENU paths (codeblock array + DEFINE MENUBAR
    DSL).

2026-04-25c

  - sample(mainmenu): new IDE-loadable sample at samples/projects/mainmenu/
    showcasing the cross-platform DEFINE MENUBAR DSL — class-based form
    (CLASS TForm1 FROM TForm) with COMPONENT ::oMenu1 TYPE CT_MAINMENU,
    File / Edit / Help popups, accelerators, and aOnClick block array
    aligned 1:1 with menu nodes (popups + separators = nil). Same source
    builds on Win32 / macOS / Linux.

  - fix(win32-ide): RestoreFormFromCode now reverse-parses DEFINE MENUBAR
    ... END MENUBAR blocks back into the chr(1)-serialized aMenuItems
    string (caption|shortcut|handler|enabled|level|parent format). Walks
    DEFINE POPUP / MENUITEM [ACTION fn(args)] [ACCEL "key"] /
    MENUSEPARATOR / END POPUP, tracks parent stack and nLevel matching
    inspector levels (popup=0, item=1, sub=2). Inspector menu editor now
    populates with the loaded items instead of showing an empty menu.
    Match strategy: by ::oMenuName from DEFINE MENUBAR, fallback to
    last CT_MAINMENU child.

  - fix(win32-ide): TMainMenu non-visual icon could not be moved on the
    form after loading a project. UI_DROPNONVISUAL created the STATIC
    HWND with SS_NOTIFY but did not subclass its WNDPROC, so the static
    absorbed WM_LBUTTONDOWN and the form's drag handler never fired.
    UI_DROPNONVISUAL now calls form->SubclassChildren() when FDesignMode
    so the new child returns HTTRANSPARENT in WM_NCHITTEST and clicks
    bubble to the form (matches the fresh-drop palette path).

  - fix(win32-ide): white flash on Scintilla when dragging the design
    form. Two root causes:
      a) SyncDesignerToCode preserved cMethods (user METHOD impls +
         static functions) across regens via RTrim(Left(cMethods,
         nLPos-1)). Harbour RTrim only strips spaces — not CR/LF — so
         a trailing \r\n accumulated each cycle (+2 bytes per click),
         making cNewCode != stored on every selection change and forcing
         a full SCI_SETTEXT round-trip. Replaced with explicit trailing
         strip of CR / LF / Space / Tab.
      b) Form drag fires OnResize continuously, regenerating cNewCode
         with new ::Left / ::Top values. SCI_SETTEXT internally
         clears+reloads the buffer and exposes the white background mid-
         operation. CODEEDITORSETTABTEXT now wraps SCI_SETTEXT with
         WM_SETREDRAW FALSE/TRUE, preserves scroll (SCI_GETFIRSTVISIBLELINE
         / SCI_GETXOFFSET) and cursor (SCI_GETCURRENTPOS / SCI_GETANCHOR
         clamped to new doc length), and ends with a non-erasing
         InvalidateRect so the repaint paints the new content over the
         old without clearing first. New SCI_* defines added.

  - fix(win32-ide): added skip-if-equal early-out at the start of
    SyncDesignerToCode (compare cNewCode to aForms[nActiveForm][3] and
    return when identical) — plain mouse clicks that don't change layout
    no longer touch Scintilla at all.

2026-04-24e (Linux — items de ListBox/ComboBox no aparecen al ejecutar ni al recargar proyecto)

  ROOT CAUSE — ITEMS NO VISIBLES EN RUNTIME NI EN PROYECTO RECARGADO:
  - RestoreFormFromCode() no parseaba la cláusula ITEMS del source .prg
    al cargar un proyecto; FItemCount quedaba en 0 y RegenerateFormCode()
    no emitía ITEMS → UserApp compilado sin items
  - HBListBox_CreateWidget(): el GtkTreeView interno no recibía
    gtk_widget_show(), quedando invisible aunque el ScrolledWindow sí
    se mostraba

  FIX (hbbuilder_linux.prg — RestoreFormFromCode):
  - Agrega parseo de cláusula ITEMS para COMBOBOX y LISTBOX igual que
    hace Windows (bucle extrae strings entre comillas, llama UI_SetProp)

  FIX (gtk3_core.c — HBListBox_CreateWidget):
  - Llama gtk_widget_show(tv) explícitamente sobre el GtkTreeView
  - Selecciona el item correcto según FItemIndex al crear el widget

2026-04-24d (Linux — items del ListBox no aparecen en runtime)

  ROOT CAUSE — ITEMS DEL LISTBOX NO VISIBLES AL EJECUTAR FORM:
  - HBListBox_CreateWidget() creaba un GtkListStore vacío y nunca leía
    FItems[] de la struct HBComboBox. A diferencia de HBComboBox_CreateWidget()
    que sí itera FItems[] al crear el widget, HBListBox_CreateWidget()
    ignoraba completamente los ítems ya almacenados en el struct.
  - Secuencia del fallo: TListBox():New() asigna FWidget=NULL →
    SetItems() llama UI_SetProp que popula FItems[] pero el bloque de
    actualización GTK se saltea (FWidget==NULL) → HBListBox_CreateWidget()
    crea el store vacío sin leer FItems[]

  FIX (gtk3_core.c — HBListBox_CreateWidget):
  - Castear HBControl* a HBComboBox* al inicio de la función
  - Iterar cb->FItems[0..cb->FItemCount-1] al crear el GtkListStore,
    igual que hace HBComboBox_CreateWidget()

2026-04-24c (Linux — crash "No exported variable" en oFont al run con ListBox/ComboBox)

  ROOT CAUSE — CRASH AL EJECUTAR FORM CON LISTBOX O COMBOBOX:
  - El generador de código Linux no tenía 'case nType == 7' para ListBox,
    por lo que caía al 'otherwise' y emitía solo un comentario; el DATA
    ::oListBox1 quedaba NIL. A continuación el generador emitía
    ::oListBox1:oFont := "Segoe UI,12", que llamaba _OFONT(NIL, ...) y
    lanzaba el error BASE/1005 "No exported variable"
  - El check de default de oFont solo excluía "System,12"; no excluía
    "Segoe UI,12" (Windows) ni "Sans,12" (Linux), emitiendo la asignación
    para absolutamente todos los controles

  FIXES EN hbbuilder_linux.prg:
  - Agrega 'case nType == 7' (ListBox): emite '@ y,x LISTBOX ::oCtrl OF
    Self SIZE w,h', con cláusula ITEMS (pipe→lista) y ':Value :=' si
    nItemIndex > 0 — mismo patrón que hbbuilder_win.prg
  - Actualiza 'case nType == 5' (ComboBox): agrega cláusula ITEMS y
    ':Value :=' (estaban ausentes en Linux, presentes en Windows)
  - oFont check: excluye "System,12", "Segoe UI,12", "Segoe UI,9" y
    "Sans,12" como valores por defecto que no deben emitirse
  - Agrega 'nVal' a las declaraciones local de RegenerateFormCode

2026-04-23c (Windows — form close during debug now pauses at Main's `return`)

  FORM CLOSE → PAUSE AT POST-RUN-LOOP USER LINE:
  - Previously when the user closed the executed form during a debug
    session, dbgclient.prg sent "DONE" and cleanly killed the subprocess
  - New behaviour: when CE_NotifyRunLoopEnded sets the flag, dbgclient
    forces DBG_RUNNING := .F. and falls through to the normal PAUSE flow
    instead of sending DONE. The subprocess then keeps executing with
    per-line PAUSE reports, and the IDE's OnDebugPause (which filters
    framework lines via nTab == 0) stops at the first user-code line
    reached after the message loop ends — typically the `return` at the
    end of Main() in Project1.prg. The user can then Step / Continue /
    Stop to finish the session with a visible end point.
  - DbgRecv poll loop: if the flag fires while the subprocess is paused
    waiting for STEP/GO, returns a synthetic "STEP" to unblock DbgHook
    without sending DONE. The next hook invocation observes the flag and
    triggers the same pause-at-next-user-line flow.

2026-04-23b (Windows — IDE responsiveness during Debug build, Debug vs Debug-to-BP split, form-close in RUNNING mode)

  ROOT CAUSE OF THE "IDE DEFORMATION" AT 125% DPI:
  - The IDE window was actually being flagged "(Not Responding)" by Windows
    during a debug build, and DWM was showing its stretched ghost bitmap —
    it was never a DPI issue at all. The cause was synchronous blocking in
    two places that stopped the IDE's message pump for several seconds.

  IDE MESSAGE PUMP STAYS ALIVE DURING DEBUG BUILD:
  - W32_ShellExec (used by every step of TBDebugRun — harbour.exe, bcc32,
    rc.exe, ilink32, copy, mkdir, etc.) no longer uses blocking ReadFile
    and WaitForSingleObject; now polls the child with PeekNamedPipe +
    MsgWaitForMultipleObjects(QS_ALLINPUT, 50 ms) so Win32 messages are
    dispatched while waiting, preventing the "(Not Responding)" mark and
    the stretched DWM ghost
  - system("taskkill /F /IM DebugApp.exe") replaced by KillDebugApp(), a
    direct Win32 API helper (CreateToolhelp32Snapshot + TerminateProcess)
    that doesn't spawn cmd.exe + taskkill.exe and returns instantly

  DEBUG vs DEBUG-TO-BP NOW BEHAVE DIFFERENTLY:
  - Debug (oRun → Debug, F8 toolbar): starts with s_dbgWasStepping = 1, so
    the session pauses at the first user-code line (classic step-through)
  - DebBP (oRun → Debug to BP, toolbar button): starts with
    s_dbgWasStepping = 0, so execution runs until the first breakpoint is
    hit (or the program ends if no BP is set)
  - IDE_DEBUGSTART2 accepts an optional third parameter lRunToBreak; the
    Harbour-side TBDebugRun passes its lRunToBreak flag through so the two
    toolbar buttons map onto the two flows

  FORM CLOSE WHILE IN FREE-RUN (after user clicked Continue):
  - dbgclient.prg: IDE_DbgRunLoopEnded() now checked at the TOP of DbgHook,
    before the RUNNING non-blocking branch. Previously the RUNNING branch
    returned early when no command was pending, so the run-loop-ended flag
    that CE_NotifyRunLoopEnded sets on WM_CLOSE was never observed and the
    debug session hung until the user clicked Stop in the IDE
  - IDE command loop: the inner RUNNING spin loop now also breaks out when
    ANY socket data arrives (not just on disconnect) so the outer loop can
    read and handle the "DONE" message the subprocess sends on form close
  - Added a process-liveness watchdog inside the RUNNING spin: uses
    OpenProcess(SYNCHRONIZE) + WaitForSingleObject(0) to detect that the
    DebugApp subprocess died (form closed + process exited before we saw
    the DONE frame) and transitions to DBG_STOPPED cleanly

2026-04-23 (Windows — Debugger ported from macOS/Linux, clickable breakpoints, form-close fix)

  DEBUGGER STATE MACHINE (ported from macOS/Linux to Windows backend):
  - Added s_dbgWasStepping flag decoupled from s_dbgState so step/breakpoint
    semantics are orthogonal; flag is set by IDE_DEBUGSTEP/STEPOVER and cleared
    by IDE_DEBUGGO (never recomputed inside the PAUSE handler)
  - Breakpoints preserved across debug sessions (removed s_nBreakpoints = 0
    reset in IDE_DEBUGSTART and IDE_DEBUGSTART2)
  - IDE_DEBUGSTART2 command loop: in RUNNING state always sends STEP (never GO)
    so subprocess pauses on every line; breakpoint/step filtering is done in
    the Harbour callback
  - IDE_DEBUGSTART2 handles "DONE" message from subprocess for clean exit when
    the executed form is closed during a pause
  - OnDebugPause (Harbour callback) skips framework lines (nTab == 0), then
    requires IDE_IsBreakpoint(cFile, nTabLine) OR IDE_DbgIsStepping() — matches
    macOS/Linux behaviour exactly, so Debug runs to first breakpoint by default

  NEW HB_FUNCs in hbbridge.cpp:
  - IDE_ISBREAKPOINT(cFile, nLine) — case-insensitive filename + line match
  - IDE_DBGISSTEPPING() — true while s_dbgWasStepping is set
  - IDE_DBGRUNLOOPENDED() — true after main form WM_CLOSE, used by dbgclient
  - IDE_DBGPUMPEVENTS() — pumps Win32 messages for ~20ms so the executed form
    stays responsive while dbgclient waits for STEP/GO from IDE
  - IDE_DEBUGPAUSEATSTEP() — no-op stub for macOS API parity
  - Extern "C" accessors IdeBpGetCount/GetModule/GetLine/Find/Add/RemoveAt so
    the CodeEditor C code can manipulate s_breakpoints[] directly

  CLICKABLE BREAKPOINTS IN CODE EDITOR:
  - Margin 1 (18px wide, to the right of line numbers) configured as a symbol
    strip showing marker 12 (red circle, SC_MARK_CIRCLE)
  - Line-number margin (margin 0) also set clickable — clicking on the line
    number itself toggles the breakpoint (VS Code style), in addition to the
    dedicated 18px breakpoint strip
  - Added missing SCI_MARKERADD/DELETE/DELETEALL/GET constants — SCI_MARKERGET
    corrected from 2047 (which is actually SCI_MARKERNEXT) to 2046, the latter
    returning -1 had caused "has marker" to always be true
  - aTabNames[MAX_TABS] added to CODEEDITOR struct so the margin-click handler
    can identify the active source file for the breakpoint entry
  - SwitchTab re-applies marker 12 to lines that have stored breakpoints after
    SCI_SETTEXT (which otherwise clears all markers)
  - CODEEDITORTOGGLEBREAKPOINT(hEd) and CODEEDITORRESTOREBREAKPOINTS(hEd,cFile)
    HB_FUNCs for the Run → "Toggle Breakpoint" / "Clear Breakpoints" menus
  - ToggleBreakpoint() Harbour stub replaced with a CodeEditorToggleBreakpoint
    call on the active tab line (the previous stub used a hard-coded line)
  - ClearBreakpoints() now also clears visible markers on the active tab

  DEBUG TOOLBAR / MENU (matches macOS/Linux):
  - Second toolbar now has: Debug, DebBP, [sep], Step, Over, Stop, Exit
    (removed the "Go" button and extra separator; Continue is accessible via
    Run → Continue menu)
  - Added Run → "Debug to BP" menu item
  - TBDebugRunToBreak() wrapper calls TBDebugRun(.T.) (same unified flow as
    Linux — both buttons share identical run-to-breakpoint behaviour)

  FORM CLOSE DURING DEBUG SESSION (main fix):
  - Clicking X on the executed form now closes it reliably; previously it
    stayed visible because DefWindowProc was not translating WM_NCLBUTTONUP
    (HTCLOSE) into WM_SYSCOMMAND(SC_CLOSE) → WM_CLOSE while the subprocess was
    in a debug pause (messages pumped via IDE_DbgPumpEvents in 20 ms slices)
  - TForm::HandleMessage now handles WM_NCLBUTTONUP with wParam == HTCLOSE
    explicitly by sending WM_CLOSE directly — bypasses DefWindowProc's
    conditional SC_CLOSE posting entirely
  - WM_CLOSE sets CE_NotifyRunLoopEnded() (hbbridge.cpp s_dbgRunLoopEnded
    flag) at the earliest point so dbgclient can exit its pause loop even if
    DestroyWindow can't run during a nested message pump
  - dbgclient.prg DbgRecv poll loop also checks IDE_DbgRunLoopEnded() every
    cycle — if the main form was closed while waiting for STEP/GO, the client
    sends "DONE" and disconnects without waiting for a hook that would never
    fire again
  - IDE-side DbgServerRecv watchdog: uses OpenProcess + WaitForSingleObject(0)
    to detect if the DebugApp subprocess died (user closed form, crash, etc.)
    and aborts polling instead of hanging on select()

  DebugApp.exe BUILD:
  - Silent link-failure detection: TBDebugRun now deletes DebugApp.exe before
    invoking ilink32/link.exe so that a stale-but-present exe can no longer
    fool the existence check (previously the IDE reported "OK" even when the
    linker silently failed, so users debugged against an out-of-date binary)
  - Added W32_ExecOpenDialog/SaveDialog/FontDialog/ColorDialog stubs in the
    generated debug_main.prg — the real implementations live in
    hbbuilder_win.obj which DebugApp does not link; without the stubs the
    link failed with unresolved externals whenever classes.prg referenced
    common dialog classes

  DebugApp.exe NO LONGER TOUCHES DPI:
  - Removed SetDPIAware() call from the _InitDPI INIT PROCEDURE that
    TBDebugRun injects into debug_main.prg
  - SETDPIAWARE HB_FUNC detects DebugApp.exe by exe filename and returns
    without calling SetProcessDPIAware, so the SetDPIAware() invocation in
    TApplication:New() (classes.prg) is also a no-op inside the subprocess
  - IDE itself is unaffected — hbbuilder_win.exe continues to call
    SetProcessDPIAware at startup as before

  KNOWN ISSUE (WINDOWS, UNRESOLVED):
  - On systems with display scaling > 100%, clicking Debug still produces a
    brief IDE visual disturbance (reported as vertical stretching at 125 %).
    All DPI calls have been removed from DebugApp.exe and none of the
    recent debugger work changes the IDE's own DPI path, so the cause is
    likely pre-existing (external console process launches, desktop
    compositor transitions) rather than introduced by these changes.

2026-04-22c (macOS — Debugger: clean exit after form closes during step mode)

  DEBUGGER CLEAN EXIT AFTER FORM CLOSE:
  - Fixed hang (spinning cursor) after closing the executed form while in step mode
  - Root cause: after form closes, debug hook fired at MAIN's final `return`; with
    s_dbgState=DBG_STEPPING the IDE paused there, blocking the subprocess indefinitely
  - Fix: subprocess now signals IDE when its [NSApp run] loop ends (form closed):
    * cocoa_core.m: calls CE_NotifyRunLoopEnded() after s_nRunLoopDepth drops to 0
    * cocoa_editor.mm: CE_NotifyRunLoopEnded() sets s_dbgRunLoopEnded flag;
      new IDE_DBGRUNLOOPENDED() HB_FUNC exposes flag to Harbour in the subprocess
    * dbgclient.prg: DbgHook() checks IDE_DbgRunLoopEnded() before sending PAUSE —
      if run loop ended, sends "DONE" and disconnects instead of blocking
    * cocoa_editor.mm (IDE side): handles "DONE" in IDE_DEBUGRUNTOBREAK2 command
      loop by breaking cleanly; resets s_dbgRunLoopEnded at session start
  - cocoa_editor_reg.c: registered IDE_DBGRUNLOOPENDED symbol for DebugApp subprocess
  - hbbuilder_macos.prg: added EXTERNAL IDE_DBGRUNLOOPENDED declaration
  - DbgRecv() already pumps Cocoa events (50ms loop with IDE_DbgPumpEvents) so the
    form remains responsive and closes cleanly while waiting for STEP/GO from IDE

2026-04-21c (Windows — IDE no longer hangs on exit while project runs)

  BUG FIX — exit-while-running:
  - Closing the IDE while a Run project (UserApp.exe) was still running
    caused the IDE window to appear DPI-deformed on screen and the
    process to hang. Closing the project first avoided it.
  - Root cause: TBRun() launched the user executable via
    W32_ShellExec('cmd /c start "" "UserApp.exe"'). W32_ShellExec
    creates an inheritable stdout/stderr pipe (bInheritHandle = TRUE on
    the SECURITY_ATTRIBUTES, only the read end explicitly stripped via
    SetHandleInformation). The intermediate cmd inherited the write
    end and — depending on how cmd's internal `start` forwarded
    bInheritHandles to CreateProcess — the grandchild UserApp could
    also inherit it. That leaked a pipe reference into the running
    user app and left the IDE with a handle tied to a process it no
    longer tracked; closing the IDE then stalled during cleanup and
    Windows DWM painted a DPI-scaled ghost bitmap of the frozen
    window (hence the "deformation").

  FIX:
  - Added HB_FUNC( W32_RUNEXE ) in source/hbbuilder_win.prg (inside
    the main BEGINDUMP block, next to W32_ShellExec). It launches the
    user exe directly via CreateProcessA with bInheritHandles = FALSE
    and DETACHED_PROCESS, so no IDE handle crosses the boundary.
    AllowSetForegroundWindow is still called so the user app can take
    focus.
  - TBRun() now calls W32_RunExe( cExePath ) on both the fast-path
    (cache-hit, no rebuild needed) and the post-build run paths —
    replacing the two `cmd /c start "" "..."` invocations.
  - W32_ShellExec remains unchanged; it is still used for all build
    commands where capturing stdout is required.

2026-04-21b (Windows — drop stubs_win.cpp, real printer APIs)

  CONSOLIDATION — stubs_win.cpp eliminated:
  - All Windows-specific HB_FUNCs previously in source/cpp/stubs_win.cpp

  - Added winspool.lib to BCC/MSVC link lines in build_win.bat and to

2026-04-21 (Windows — Report PDF writer, build-assembly Chr(26) fix)

  NATIVE WINDOWS PDF WRITER:
  - Replaced the RPT_PDF* stub functions in source/cpp/stubs_win.cpp with
    a real PDF 1.4 writer. No external dependencies — emits PDF bytes
    directly (catalog, pages tree, content streams, xref, trailer).
  - RPT_PDFOPEN / RPT_PDFADDPAGE / RPT_PDFDRAWRECT / RPT_PDFDRAWTEXT /
    RPT_EXPORTPDF now render filled/stroked rectangles and text with
    font/size/bold/italic/color, matching the Linux (Cairo) and macOS
    (Core Graphics) backends.
  - Maps incoming font family names (Arial/Helvetica/Times/Courier/Mono/
    Consolas/etc.) to one of the PDF standard 14 core fonts with
    bold/italic variants. WinAnsi encoding is compatible with Harbour's
    default CP_ACP on Windows.
  - Screen coordinates (Y-down) are flipped to PDF's bottom-left origin.
  - Fixes linker error: Unresolved external '_HB_FUN_RPT_PDFDRAWRECT'
    referenced from HBBUILDER_WIN.OBJ. Calling classes.prg:2736 inside
    TReport:ExportPDF() no longer fails to link.

  USER-PROJECT BUILD: STRIP EMBEDDED Chr(26) FROM main.prg:
  - Form files saved via MemoWrit carry a trailing Chr(26) (DOS EOF).
    When the IDE concatenated Project1.prg + Form*.prg into the assembled
    main.prg, those embedded ^Z bytes silently truncated Harbour's view
    of the file at the first occurrence — dropping the entire
    #pragma BEGINDUMP/ENDDUMP block that defines the platform-stub
    HB_FUN_* symbols.
  - Symptom: link failed with 14 unresolved externals on UserApp.exe
    (UI_MEMONEW, UI_MSGBOX, UI_MSGYESNO, UI_SCENE3DNEW, UI_EARTHVIEWNEW,
    UI_MAPNEW, UI_MAPSETREGION, UI_MAPADDPIN, UI_MAPCLEARPINS,
    UI_MASKEDITNEW, UI_STRINGGRIDNEW, UI_GRIDSETCELL, UI_GRIDGETCELL,
    W32_ERRORDIALOG).
  - Fix: TBRun and TBDebug now strip Chr(26) from cAllPrg right before
    writing main.prg / debug_main.prg, so Harbour sees the full text
    including the BEGINDUMP block.

2026-04-20c (macOS — TSQLite cursor navigation, DBGrid nAlign, inspector fixes)

  TSQLite — CURSOR NAVIGATION FOR DBGRID:
  - Added cTable, cSQL, aRows, aFieldNames, nRecord fields to TSQLite.
  - New methods: FieldCount(), FieldName(n), GoTop(), Eof(), FieldGet(n),
    Skip(n), LoadCursor() — enables DBGrid to use TSQLite as datasource.
  - Open() now calls LoadCursor() automatically when cTable or cSQL is set.
  - LoadCursor() runs SELECT * FROM cTable (or custom cSQL) and caches all
    rows in aRows using sqlite3_prepare/sqlite3_step/sqlite3_finalize.
  - LoadFromDataSource() auto-calls LoadCursor() if connected but cursor
    not yet loaded (handles case where cTable is set after Open()).
  - LoadFromDataSource() auto-calls Open() if component not yet connected.
  - NULL SQLite values converted to "" (sqlite3_column_text returns nil
    for SQL NULL; now guarded with iif(xCol==nil,"",hb_ValToStr(xCol))).

  CRASH FIX — UI_DBGridSetCache nil string:
  - [NSString stringWithUTF8String:sz] returns nil for invalid UTF-8 data
    (e.g. binary SQLite columns), causing [NSMutableArray addObject:nil]
    crash. Added Latin-1 fallback; if both fail, uses @"".

  TSQLite INSPECTOR PROPERTIES:
  - Added cTable (table name), cSQL (custom query), lActive (auto-open)
    to CT_SQLITE inspector panel under "Data" / "Behavior" categories.
  - FTable[64] and FSQL[512] fields added to HBControl struct.
  - UI_GetProp / UI_SetProp handlers added for cTable and cSQL.
  - IDE code generation emits cTable, cSQL, and Open() (when lActive)
    in the correct order before DBGrid LoadFromDataSource.

  INSPECTOR — SQLite cFileName file picker:
  - cFileName picker no longer forces *.dbf filter for all controls.
  - For TDBFTable: keeps *.dbf filter and "Select DBF File" title.
  - For TSQLite and others: allows all files, no extension restriction.
  - szClassName[64] added to INSDATA; set in INS_RefreshWithData so
    openFilePickerForRow can check control type without C struct access.

  DBGRID nAlign / alClient LAYOUT (macOS designer):
  - Setting nAlign on a DBGrid now correctly updates FDockAlign (layout
    engine field) in addition to FGridAlign (display field).
  - ApplyDockAlign() called immediately when nAlign changes, updating
    the NSView frame in real time in both design and runtime modes.
  - Fix was in the generic nAlign handler (line 5705) which was
    intercepting DBGrid nAlign before the type-specific handler.
  - UI_FormRebuildChildren now calls ApplyDockAlign() after
    createAllChildren so alignment is applied when reopening a project.

2026-04-17 (macOS: Smart Cut/Copy/Paste + paste renders controls)

  FEATURES
  - Toolbar Cut/Copy/Paste buttons and Edit menu now route through
    SmartCut() / SmartCopy() / SmartPaste(): when the form designer is the
    key window and has selected controls, operations act on those controls;
    otherwise they delegate to the code editor.
  - SmartCut() saves an undo snapshot before deleting the cut controls.
  - Added UI_FormSelCount( hForm ) HB_FUNC to query the number of selected
    controls from Harbour code.
  - Added UI_FormDeleteSelected( hForm ) HB_FUNC to remove selected controls
    from the form (view + child array + global registry).

    HBControl object but never called createViewInParent:, so no NSView was
    built. Fixed by calling createViewInParent: after addChild: for each
    pasted control.
