2026-04-17 (macOS: Undo/Redo wired to toolbar buttons + design undo fixes)

  FEATURES
  - Toolbar Undo/Redo buttons and Edit menu Redo now route through SmartUndo()
    / SmartRedo(): Undo checks the design-undo stack first and falls back to
    the code-editor undo; Redo delegates to the code editor (design redo stack
    not yet implemented).

  FIXES
  - UndoPushSnapshot forward declaration was placed before the HBForm
    @interface, causing the compiler to resolve HBForm* to the deprecated
    AppKit NSForm class and emit a "conflicting types" error. Moved the
    forward declaration to after the HBForm @interface definition.
  - UI_FormUndo was decrementing the stack pointer before restoring the
    snapshot, so it restored from an uninitialised slot. Fixed restore-then-
    decrement order.
  - UndoPushSnapshot was never called before drag-move or resize operations,
    so those actions could not be undone. Push is now performed in mouseDown
    before both resize and drag paths.
  - Cmd+Z was wired directly to CodeEditorUndo; replaced with SmartUndo()
    so the designer undo stack is drained first.

2026-04-17 (macOS: TDBGrid — cell content visible at runtime from datasource)

  FEATURES
  - TDBGrid now displays live data from a connected datasource (TDBFTable,
    TCompArray, etc.) when the form runs. LoadFromDataSource() reads all
    records into a Harbour array and passes them to the Cocoa layer via
    UI_DBGridSetCache before Activate() is called.

  FIXES
  - HBBrowseDelegate (NSTableView datasource/delegate) was stored only as a
    local variable; NSTableView holds delegates as weak references so ARC
    deallocated it before the window appeared. Added a strong reference in
    BrowseData.delegate to keep it alive.
  - loadAllDBGrids was only called in the "window already exists" path of
    createWindowWithRunLoop:. New windows (first Activate) never flushed
    FPendingRowData into rowData. Fixed by calling loadAllDBGrids after
    createAllChildren in both code paths.
  - FlushPendingDBGrids now recurses through the full child subtree so
    DBGrids nested inside panels/containers are also populated.
  - RegenerateFormCode defers LoadFromDataSource() calls to the end of the
    generated CreateForm() method so all datasource components are fully
    constructed before the grid tries to read from them.

2026-04-16 (Windows: Inspector enum dropdown — TrackPopupMenu + BorderStyle codegen)

  FIXES
  - Inspector enum dropdowns (nBorderStyle, nCursor, nAlignment, etc.) could
    not be used reliably: the in-place ComboBox child of the ListView lost
    focus immediately (WM_KILLFOCUS fired before the user could interact)
    because the ListView parent reclaimed focus after NM_CLICK handling.
    Replaced the in-place ComboBox with TrackPopupMenu — the same reliable
    approach already used for boolean properties. The popup menu appears
    below the value cell, checkmarks the current value, and commits
    immediately on selection with no focus issues.
  - After selecting an enum value the Inspector row was not repainted to
    show the new string name. Added InsRebuild() call after InsApplyValue()
    in the TrackPopupMenu path (mirrors the existing boolean handler).
  - RegenerateFormCode (Windows) did not emit ::BorderStyle when nBorderStyle
    != 2 (bsSizeable). Running a project that had bsDialog/bsSingle/etc. set
    in the designer always produced a resizable window because the generated
    .prg code never assigned the property. Now emits
    "   ::BorderStyle := N" for any non-default value, matching the macOS
    backend behaviour.

2026-04-16 (Windows: TForm nBorderStyle — bsDialog + enum display fix)

  FIXES
  - Inspector dropdown for nBorderStyle was missing bsDialog and
    bsSizeToolWin, and had the wrong item order (bsSizeable at index 0
    instead of bsNone). Fixed s_borderStyle array in
    inspector/inspector_win.prg to match the hbbuilder.ch constants:
    index 0=bsNone, 1=bsSingle, 2=bsSizeable, 3=bsDialog,
    4=bsToolWindow, 5=bsSizeToolWin (nCount 4→6).
  - TForm::CreateHandle (tform.cpp) ignored FBorderStyle entirely and
    used the legacy FSizable/FToolWindow flags. Replaced with a switch
    on FBorderStyle so bsNone/bsSingle/bsDialog/bsToolWindow/
    bsSizeToolWin all produce the correct Win32 style flags at creation.
    FBorderStyle default changed from 0 to 2 (bsSizeable) to match the
    Delphi/C++Builder convention and the macOS backend.
  - When nBorderStyle is changed live in the Inspector while the design
    window is already open, hbbridge.cpp now applies SetWindowLongPtr +
    SWP_FRAMECHANGED immediately, the same way macOS applies
    applyStyleMask. Previously the change was stored but not reflected
    until the form was recreated.
  - All 12 numeric ENUMDEF properties (nBorderStyle, nPosition,
    nWindowState, nFormStyle, nCursor, nBevelStyle, nBevelOuter,
    nAlignment, nScrollBars, nShapeType, nViewStyle, nBorderIcons)
    were displayed as raw integers in the Inspector value column. Fixed
    InsRebuild (both full-rebuild and partial-update paths) to resolve
    the numeric index to its ENUMDEF string name before rendering.

2026-04-16 (Windows: fix ListBox/ComboBox nItemIndex inspector + runtime)

  FIXES
  - Inspector showed "0" after typing "1" into nItemIndex for ListBox or
    ComboBox. Root cause: OnPropChanged (fired from InsEndEdit via
    InsApplyValue) was calling InspectorRefresh, which triggered
    INS_RefreshWithData resetting d->nRows=0 and rebuilding all property
    rows. The stale nReal index InsEndEdit still held then caused
    WM_KILLFOCUS to re-enter InsEndEdit with d->nEditRow=-1, clobbering
    the displayed value. Fix: removed InspectorRefresh from OnPropChanged.
    The inspector cell repaints correctly from d->rows[nReal].szValue once
    d->hEdit is destroyed — no explicit refresh needed.
  - Runtime: selected item was not restored when running a project that had
    nItemIndex > 0 set in the designer. Added UI_SetProp case for ComboBox
    nItemIndex (was missing — only GET existed). Unified FItemIndex to
    1-based convention across TListBox and TComboBox (1 = first item,
    0 = nothing selected). TComboBox::CreateHandle and SetItemIndex now
    apply FItemIndex-1 as the CB_SETCURSEL index. Codegen emits
    "::oCtrl:Value := N" as a separate line after the @ COMBOBOX/LISTBOX
    line; RestoreFormFromCode parses those lines to reload FItemIndex into
    the designer on re-open.

2026-04-16 (macOS: Media tab — TMap / TScene3D / TEarthView)

  FEATURES
  - New palette tab "Media" for embedded rich content. Three controls
    in this initial drop:
  - TMap (CT_MAP=140): MapKit-backed map viewer. Properties Lat, Lon,
    Zoom (1..20), MapType (mtStandard/mtSatellite/mtHybrid/
    mtMutedStandard). Methods SetRegion, AddPin (lat, lon, title,
    subtitle), ClearPins. Uses Apple Maps data — free, no API key.
    MAP command + codegen/parser. Constants mtStandard..mtMutedStandard
    in hbbuilder.ch.
  - TScene3D (CT_SCENE3D=141): SceneKit-backed 3D viewer. Loads
    .usdz / .usd / .dae / .scn / .obj via cSceneFile (alias Picture)
    with NSImageScaleProportionallyUpOrDown. allowsCameraControl=YES
    (orbit/zoom/pan with mouse + trackpad), autoenablesDefaultLighting.
    Default placeholder when no file is loaded: a slowly rotating
    blue dodecahedron built from scratch via HBBuildRotatingDodecahedron
    (20 vertices, 12 pentagonal faces fan-triangulated to 36 triangles
    with per-face normals, blue Phong material, Y-axis rotation
    SCNAction repeated forever — 8s per turn). SCENE3D command +
    codegen/parser. Inspector file picker filters by 3D extensions.
  - TEarthView (CT_EARTHVIEW=142): globe-style satellite Earth view.
    MKMapView with mapType=Satellite and a high-altitude MKMapCamera
    (30,000 km) — at this distance modern MapKit renders Earth's
    curvature, giving a real globe view with live Apple Maps imagery.
    Auto-rotation via NSTimer (HBEarthRotator) advancing the camera
    center longitude every 50ms (~9°/sec). Skipped in design mode so
    coordinates don't mutate while editing. Properties Lat, Lon,
    lAutoRotate. EARTHVIEW command + codegen/parser. Palette icon
    composited from SF Symbol globe.americas.fill.
  - Palette icons: TMap (map.fill), TScene3D (cube.transparent.fill),
    TEarthView (globe.americas.fill) all composited over the same
    18px-tall light-grey pill so they match the visual weight of the
    existing BMP icons.
  - Sample projects under samples/projects/: scene3D (model loader
    with Load/Clear/About), maps (city jumps, AddPin demo with 8
    world capitals, MapType cycle), earth (auto-rotating globe with
    Pause/Resume + Madrid/Tokyo/NewYork/Sydney jumps). All in IDE-
    canonical format (CLASS TFormN FROM TForm + METHOD CreateForm).

  FIXES
  - createAllChildren was filtering all controls with FControlType >=
    CT_TIMER (38) at runtime, intended to skip non-visual components
    (Timer, OpenDialog, DBFTable...) but actually hiding every visual
    control added later: TWebView=62, TBrowse/DB family (79..86),
    TMap=140, TScene3D=141, TEarthView=142. Replaced the blanket >=
    CT_TIMER filter with an explicit isVisualHigh allow-list.
    Without this, dropping any of these controls onto a form
    showed nothing on Run.
  - User-project linker (Build action in the IDE) was missing
    -framework MapKit / CoreLocation / SceneKit, causing undefined
    symbol errors when a project used TMap, TScene3D or TEarthView.
    Both invocations in source/hbbuilder_macos.prg and the default
    string in the Project Options dialog (cocoa_editor.mm) updated.
  - EARTHVIEW codegen used Str(num, 10, 6) which overflows to
    "**********" for longitudes wider than 10 chars (e.g.
    -179.999999 needs 11). Bumped to Str(num, 14, 6).
  - TEarthView no longer auto-rotates in design mode — the timer
    mutated FLon continuously, which the codegen then wrote to the
    .prg at every save. Now FCtrlParent->FDesignMode is checked and
    the timer is only scheduled at runtime.
  - Setting the bd->tableView column width via [cols objectAtIndex:]
    needed an explicit (NSTableColumn *) cast — SceneKit introduced
    multiple setWidth: methods that made the message ambiguous on id.

2026-04-16 (macOS: TShape/TBevel/TMaskEdit/TStringGrid real implementations)

  FEATURES
  - TShape: full geometric primitive. New HBShapeView (NSBezierPath)
    renders stRectangle, stSquare, stRoundRect, stRoundSquare,
    stEllipse, stCircle. nClrPane acts as fill, new nPenColor and
    nPenWidth control the stroke. Defaults: solid white fill, black
    1px pen, stRectangle — applied both from UI_ShapeNew and from
    palette drop. SHAPE command + codegen/parser round-trip.
    Constants stRectangle..stCircle in hbbuilder.ch.
  - TBevel: 3D beveled primitive with Delphi parity. New HBBevelView
    renders bsBox, bsFrame, bsTopLine, bsBottomLine, bsLeftLine,
    bsRightLine, bsSpacer with bvLowered / bvRaised styles. Uses 2px
    light+dark lines for the 3D effect. BEVEL command (with SHAPE
    and STYLE clauses) + codegen/parser. Constants bsBox..bsSpacer
    and bvLowered/bvRaised in hbbuilder.ch.
  - TMaskEdit: live masked input with Delphi-style character classes
    ('0', '9', '#' digits; 'L', 'l' letters; 'A', 'a' alphanumeric;
    anything else literal). New HBMaskEditDelegate reformats on
    controlTextDidChange:, auto-inserting literals between edit slots
    so users type "12" for a date mask and see "12/". The mask
    template ("__/__/____") is shown as grey placeholder when the
    field is empty. New nMaskKind enum of presets: meDate, meDateISO,
    meTime, meTimeSecs, mePhone, meZipCode, meCreditCard, meSSN,
    meIPv4 — setting the kind auto-fills cEditMask. TMaskEdit:New
    accepts either a mask string or a preset number. MASKEDIT
    command + codegen that emits the preset constant name when set.
  - TStringGrid: real matrix control. New HBStringGridDataSource
    (NSTableViewDataSource + Delegate) backed by NSMutableArray of
    NSMutableArray<NSString*>. Properties nColCount, nRowCount,
    nFixedRows (default 1, serves as header row), nFixedCols (default
    0) exposed in the Inspector. Fixed rows/cols are non-editable,
    rendered with light-grey background + bold font. New HB_FUNCs
    UI_StringGridNew, UI_GridSetCell, UI_GridGetCell. Resizing the
    grid preserves existing content. TStringGrid class with
    ColCount, RowCount, FixedRows, FixedCols, and 1-based
    SetCell/GetCell methods. STRINGGRID command + codegen/parser.
  - Palette icons: UI_PaletteLoadImages now composites better icons
    for selected controls on macOS 11+ using SF Symbols. TMaskEdit
    gets a composed icon: a low-profile (18px tall) rounded light-
    grey pill + dark textformat.123 glyph, matching the visual
    height of the existing BMP icons.

2026-04-16 (macOS: TBitBtn/TSpeedButton/TImage with Kind+Picture, SpeedButton palette fix)

  FEATURES
  - TBitBtn: full C++Builder parity on macOS. Properties Kind
    (bkCustom..bkAll), cPicture, Glyph (alias), ModalResult,
    Default, Cancel. Kind auto-populates Caption + ModalResult
    (bkOK -> "OK"+mrOk, bkCancel -> "Cancel"+mrCancel, etc.).
    Images resolved via SF Symbols on macOS 11+ when Kind is set
    and cPicture is empty (checkmark.circle.fill for bkOK, etc.).
    New BITBTN command:
        @ T, L BITBTN ::oCtrl [PROMPT c] OF parent SIZE W, H
                       [KIND n] [PICTURE cPath]
    Codegen + parser round-trip; inspector exposes nKind (dropdown),
    cPicture (file picker), nModalResult.
  - TSpeedButton: dedicated class, backend function UI_SpeedBtnNew,
    SPEEDBUTTON command mirroring BITBTN. Delphi-style defaults on
    creation: btnFace background (0x00F0F0F0) and Flat=False so a
    1px grey border with cornerRadius=3 appears by default. Flat
    property toggles the border live. Palette drop also applies
    these defaults so dragging from the palette produces the
    expected look, not an invisible button.
  - TImage: class with cPicture/Picture properties; backend loads
    NSImage from the path in createViewInParent and applies
    NSImageScaleProportionallyUpOrDown. UI_SetProp("cPicture") or
    ("cFileName") on CT_IMAGE reloads the live image. New IMAGE
    command; codegen + parser. Inspector file picker now filters by
    image extensions (png/jpg/jpeg/gif/bmp/tiff/tif/icns) when the
    row is cPicture.
  - Constants in hbbuilder.ch: clBtnFace, clBtnShadow, clBlack,
    clWhite, clRed, clGreen, clBlue (BGR byte order, C++Builder
    system color parity); bkCustom..bkAll; mrNone..mrClose.
  - nClrPane now applies to buttons (CT_BUTTON, CT_BITBTN,
    CT_SPEEDBTN). NSButton ignores backgroundColor, so the setter
    routes through wantsLayer + layer.backgroundColor.

  FIXES
  - SpeedButton palette type mismatch: the palette registered
    TSpeedButton with type 27, but CT_SPEEDBTN is 13. Dropping from
    the palette produced nothing because the dispatcher in
    OnComponentDrop couldn't find the type in its defs[] table.
    Changed the palette registration to 13.
  - BITBTN command emission was broken when only KIND or only
    PICTURE was present. Harbour's `[; ... ]` output gating does
    NOT suppress the line when its marker is absent; it emits the
    line with the marker replaced by empty, producing
    "::oBtn:cPicture := " with no RHS (E0020 Incomplete statement).
    Rewrote the xcommand to pass optional values as positional
    args to TBitBtn():New(), which Harbour does accept as empty
    (`,,`). TBitBtn:New applies each only when non-nil. Same
    pattern for SPEEDBUTTON and IMAGE.
  - Codegen nClrPane bug: the condition "nCtrlClr != 4294967295
    .and. nCtrlClr != 0" excluded pure black (0) from being
    emitted. Now only the sentinel 0xFFFFFFFF is suppressed.

2026-04-16 (macOS: CheckBox/RadioButton CHECKED persistence, codegen robustness)

  FEATURES
  - CHECKBOX / RADIOBUTTON codegen now emits the CHECKED clause when
    lChecked is true in the designer, and the form-loader parses
    " CHECKED" back into UI_SetProp("lChecked", .T.). Runtime state
    now matches what the user sees in the Inspector.
  - TRadioButton lChecked fully wired on macOS: new FRadioChecked
    field on HBControl (default NO) persists the checked state even
    when UI_SetProp is called before the NSButton exists. Applied
    in createViewInParent on the CT_RADIO branch, mirroring the
    HBCheckBox FChecked pattern.
  - TRadioButton Checked exposed in the Inspector: UI_GetAllProps
    adds an lChecked row for CT_RADIO reading the live NSButton
    state (or FRadioChecked when the view isn't created yet).
  - UI_GetProp / UI_SetProp now handle "lChecked" on CT_RADIO
    (previously only CT_CHECKBOX), so ::oRadio:Checked works both
    at design-time and runtime.

  FIXES
  - Codegen no longer emits property assignments for controls
    whose creation line was only a comment placeholder. For types
    without a dedicated case (TScrollBar, TPanel, TBevel, TShape,
    TImage, TBitBtn, TSpeedButton, TMaskEdit, TStringGrid,
    TScrollBox, TStaticText, TLabeledEdit, TListView, TProgressBar,
    TRichEdit, TTrackBar, TUpDown, TDateTimePicker, TMonthCalendar,
    TPaintBox, TWebView), RegenerateFormCode emits
        // ::oCtrl (TScrollBar) at L,T SIZE W,H
    followed by an empty DATA slot — and previously also emitted
    ::oCtrl:oFont := "...", ::oCtrl:nClrPane := N, etc. At runtime
    those assignments sent messages to a nil DATA, which Harbour
    reported as "No exported variable" (BASE 1005, Operation OFONT).
    A new lCommented flag is set in the commented-only branch and
    the property-emit section is skipped via `loop`.

2026-04-16 (macOS: TListBox/TComboBox aItems+nItemIndex, TForm nBorderStyle live update)

  FEATURES
  - TListBox: new aItems property exposed in the Inspector as an
    editable array (same popup used by TTreeView). Backed by FHeaders;
    an HBListBoxDataSource mirrors the pipe-separated string into a
    flat NSTableView row list. The LISTBOX command in hbbuilder.ch
    accepts an ITEMS clause; codegen emits and the parser restores it
    from the generated .prg.
  - TListBox: new nItemIndex property (1-based, default 1, valid
    range 1..count, 0 = no selection). Reading via UI_GetProp,
    writing via UI_SetProp, round-trips the NSTableView selection.
    HBListBoxDataSource now also acts as NSTableViewDelegate and
    fires OnChange with the 1-based index on user selection.
  - TComboBox: aItems property exposed in the Inspector. FHeaders
    is the source of truth; when set, FItems[] and the NSPopUpButton
    are rebuilt. UI_ComboAddItem now also appends to FHeaders so the
    two stay in sync with incremental additions from code.
  - TComboBox: nItemIndex is 1-based like TListBox (default 1,
    0 = no selection). New UI_SetProp handler for CT_COMBOBOX
    converts 1↔0 at the NSPopUpButton boundary. TComboBox:Value
    ASSIGN now routes through UI_SetProp so the round-trip is
    consistent.
  - TForm nBorderStyle: the style mask is now computed by a new
    -[HBForm computeStyleMask] helper and applied live via
    -[HBForm applyStyleMask]. Setting nBorderStyle, nBorderIcons,
    lToolWindow or lAppBar in the Inspector updates the window
    immediately without needing to reopen the form.
  - TForm bsToolWindow / bsSizeToolWin: macOS honors
    NSWindowStyleMaskUtilityWindow only on NSPanel, so tool windows
    are now instantiated as NSPanel (setFloatingPanel:YES). A live
    change between bsToolWindow and the other styles recreates the
    window in applyStyleMask, preserving contentView, title, frame
    and background color.
  - nBorderStyle persistence: GenerateFormCode emits
    `::BorderStyle := N` when not bsSizeable, and RestoreFormFromCode
    recognizes the line and applies it via UI_SetProp. Runtime now
    honors the value chosen in the designer.

  FIXES
  - nBorderStyle=bsDialog (and other non-resizable styles) now
    actually prevents resizing. setStyleMask alone is unreliable
    on already-visible NSWindows, so applyStyleMask also pins
    minSize = maxSize = frame.size and hides the resize indicator
    when the mask lacks NSWindowStyleMaskResizable. Restores
    sensible min/unlimited max on resizable styles.
  - applyStyleMask is now called at the end of createWindowWithRunLoop
    so the min/max pinning is in place from the first frame the user
    sees at runtime (previously the runtime window was briefly
    non-resizable but then reverted to the default geometry
    constraints).

2026-04-15 (macOS: Inspector logical dropdown fix)

  FIXES
  - Object Inspector: setting a logical property to .F. via the
    Yes/No dropdown now persists. The logical dropdown previously
    read [NSMenuItem isHighlighted] after the popup had closed,
    which is unreliable — selecting "No" often left the value
    unchanged. Switched to the same action-selector pattern used
    by the regular dropdown (dropdownMenuSelected: + s_dropdownChoice),
    so mouse selection of .T./.F. works consistently for
    lTransparent and any other logical property.

2026-04-15 (Linux/GTK3: Inspector properties, AppTitle, Reopen Last Project, TFolder/TPageControl)

  FEATURES
  - Inspector properties exposed for Label/Edit/StaticText/MaskEdit/
    LabeledEdit: nClrText (foreground color), nAlign (0=Left,1=Center,
    2=Right) applied via gtk_label_set_xalign / gtk_entry_set_alignment.
    Label additionally gets lTransparent; when false + nClrPane is set
    a background is painted via CSS USER-priority provider.
  - AppTitle property on TForm (cAppTitle) shown in the Inspector.
    Codegen emits `::AppTitle := "..."` and load parser restores it
    from saved source.
  - File menu: "Reopen Last Project" reopens the most recent .hbp via
    [Recent] File1..File8 entries in hbbuilder.ini. IniRead/IniWrite
    are now key-preserving so the DarkMode + Recent entries coexist.
  - TFolder / TPageControl (CT_TABCONTROL2): new backend infrastructure.
    HBTabControl2 struct (FTabs, FPageCount); SetTabs builds a real
    GtkNotebook with per-page GtkFixed bodies. Per-control page
    ownership via FPageOwner/FPageIndex, applied by HBControl_AddChild
    through a pending-owner mechanism (set by TFolderPage:hCpp or by
    the designer when a palette drop lands inside a folder).
  - Palette drop routing: dropping a non-folder control inside a
    folder's bounds auto-tags the new control with FPageOwner + active
    page so it becomes part of the current tab. Palette entry for
    CT_TABCONTROL2 renamed to "Folder" (TFolder).
  - Codegen: RegenerateFormCode collects a child→name map and emits
    FOLDER command with PROMPTS plus "OF ::oFolder:aPages[N]" for each
    paged child; RestoreFormFromCode parses both, calling
    UI_SetPendingPageOwner before creating the child.
  - Inspector: folder-page sub-entries "oFolderN:aPages[M] AS
    TFolderPage /* Tab text */" in the combo; selecting one switches
    the active tab (UI_TabControlSetSel) and shows cCaption/nPage in
    the inspector. New HB_FUNCs INS_SetFolderPage, INS_AddRow,
    INS_AddCategoryRow, INS_Rebuild in the GTK inspector.
  - OnComponentDrop seeds a fresh folder with default aTabs
    ("Tab 1|Tab 2|Tab 3") so both runtime and codegen have visible
    tabs immediately after the drop.
  - HBForm_HitTestControl skips children whose widget is hidden or
    lives on an inactive folder page so selection behaves.
  - HBForm_CreateAllChildren creates folders before other controls
    and routes paged children into their page's GtkFixed with coords
    translated from form-absolute to page-relative (minus tab strip).

  FIXES
  - Critical heap-corruption fix in UI_GetAllProps. The ADD_S/N/L/C/F
    macros were multi-statement but not wrapped in do{...}while(0);
    `if( cond ) ADD_L(...);` left subsequent statements executing
    unconditionally, causing hb_itemRelease on an already-released
    PHB_ITEM ("malloc(): unaligned fastbin chunk detected"). Fixed
    by bracing all conditional ADD_* usages.
  - on_tab_switch_page: the GtkNotebook "switch-page" signal fires
    while gtk_notebook_get_current_page still returns the OLD page.
    Switched to using the nPageIdx signal parameter so visibility
    updates track the destination tab (was causing the 3→2 case to
    not show the page-2 control).
  - Menu bitmap positions in File menu shifted by +1 after adding
    "Reopen Last Project" so Exit shows menu_exit.png again, etc.
  - TFolder runtime click routing: paged children now live inside the
    notebook page's GtkFixed. Previously they were form-level with
    manual show/hide, which made gtk_widget_show leave them behind
    the notebook's event grab so button clicks stopped firing after
    tab1 → tab2 → tab1. GTK now handles visibility + events natively.

  FILES CHANGED

  - source/backends/gtk3/gtk3_inspector.c
  - source/hbbuilder_linux.prg
  - source/inspector/inspector_gtk.prg

2026-04-15 (iOS: native UIKit backend, IDE integration, form designer fixes)

  FEATURES
  - iOS backend: new source/backends/ios/ with native UIKit controls.
    Implements the same UI_* API as the Android backend (UI_FormNew,
    UI_LabelNew, UI_ButtonNew, UI_EditNew, UI_SetText, UI_GetText,
    UI_OnClick, UI_SetFormColor, UI_SetCtrlColor, UI_SetCtrlFont).
    Controls are real UILabel, UIButton, UITextField — no WebView.
  - Harbour for iOS: cross-compiled Harbour 3.2.0dev for iOS arm64
    (device) and x86_64 (simulator) with minimal patches (3 files
    guarded for system() unavailability on iOS + auto-detection of
    HB_OS_IOS via TargetConditionals.h).
  - build-ios-app.sh: 4-stage build pipeline (PRG→C, cross-compile,
    link with Harbour iOS libs + UIKit frameworks, create signed .app
    bundle with Info.plist). Supports both device and simulator targets.
  - bootstrap-harbour.sh: cross-compiles Harbour source for iOS arm64
    or x86_64 simulator, mirroring the Android bootstrap script.
  - setup-ios-toolchain.sh: verifies Xcode, iOS SDK, simulator runtime,
    and Harbour iOS libs; offers to install missing components.
  - install-and-run.sh: installs .app on iOS simulator and launches it.
  - "Run on iOS..." menu item in macOS IDE: generates UI_* PRG code
    from the visual form design, builds .app via build-ios-app.sh,
    and installs/launches on the iPhone Simulator.
  - "iOS Setup Wizard..." menu item in macOS IDE: checks toolchain
    status (Xcode, iOS SDK, simulator, Harbour host, Harbour iOS libs)
    and offers to run setup-ios-toolchain.sh in Terminal.app.
  - GenerateiOSPRG(): converts visual form design to UI_* API calls
    for iOS target, with 50px vertical offset for safe area, proper
    control type mapping (Label/Edit/Button), and button click handlers.
  - iOS sample project: samples/projects/ios/ with Project1.prg,
    Form1.prg, Project1.hbp, and README.md.
  - iOS platform documentation: docs/en/platform-ios.html,
    docs/es/platform-ios.html, and docs/pt/platform-ios.html.
  - Android platform docs in Portuguese: docs/pt/platform-android.html.
  - Updated landing page (docs/index.html) with iOS availability.
  - harbour-ios-arm64.zip: pre-built Harbour iOS libraries in releases/.
  - iOS backend copied to app bundle via build_mac.sh.

  FIXES
  - macOS form designer: buttons now resize correctly with the rubber
    band. Changed from NSBezelStyleRounded (which constrains height to
    intrinsic content size) to NSBezelStyleRegularSquare with layer-based
    rounded corners (cornerRadius=6), so the button respects explicit
    frame dimensions from resize handles.
  - iOS button styling: light gray background (0.82,0.82,0.84) with
    black text and rounded corners, matching the macOS form designer.
  - GenerateiOSPRG: fixed swapped control types (nType==2 is Edit,
    nType==3 is Button), fixed cVarName→cName property name, fixed
    UI_GetProp("nType")→UI_GetType() API, and only binds UI_OnClick
    for buttons to prevent undefined symbol linker errors.

2026-04-14 (macOS: Label OnClick, button caption update, nClrPane fixes)

  FEATURES
  - TLabel OnClick: labels now fire the OnClick event at runtime via
    NSClickGestureRecognizer on the NSTextField view.
  - TButton caption: changing cText in the inspector now updates the
    button's visible title immediately (previously setStringValue: was
    called instead of setTitle: because NSButton responds to both but
    only setTitle: updates the displayed caption).

  FIXES
  - nClrPane accumulation on labels: changing a label's background color
    no longer duplicates `::oLabel1:nClrPane := ...` lines in generated
    code. Properties managed by codegen (nClrPane, lTransparent, nAlign,
    oFont) are now excluded from the generic "preserve ::oCtrl:xxx :="
    scan that caused duplicates when values changed between regenerations.
  - nClrPane not visible on labels at runtime: when nClrPane was set
    before the view was created (the normal runtime order), the label
    stayed transparent because createViewInParent always used
    drawsBackground:!FTransparent. Now createViewInParent checks
    FClrPane and enables drawsBackground + applies FBgColor when a
    custom color was set. UI_SETPROP also forces drawsBackground:YES
    when nClrPane changes on an existing NSTextField.
  - Event wiring dedup: control-level and form-level event scans now
    check cEvents before adding, preventing duplicate ::OnClick lines
    when the same event wiring exists in both the generic preserve scan
    and the event-specific scan.

2026-04-14 (macOS: nAlign, METHOD dedup, non-visual guards, menu icons, New App fix)

  FEATURES
  - TLabel and TEdit now support nAlign property (0=Left, 1=Center, 2=Right).
    Inspector shows a dropdown with Left|Center|Right. The alignment maps
    correctly to macOS NSTextAlignment (where Right=1, Center=2 in the enum,
    opposite to our convention).
  - Reopen Last Project: File > Reopen Last Project reopens the most recent
    .hbp from the INI-backed recent list (up to 8 entries, deduped).
  - Event handler codegen now detects whether a handler is a METHOD of the
    form class (uses ::Method() send) or a standalone function (uses
    FuncName(Self) call), matching the C++Builder/RadStudio pattern.
  - Form-level event detection: OnCreate, OnShow, OnClose, OnResize, etc.
    are now scanned and wired when their handler exists in the code.

  FIXES
  - METHOD accumulation: repeated form moves/resizes no longer duplicate
    METHOD declarations inside the CLASS body. Both the external-implementation
    scan and the inline-declaration scan now collect into a shared aMethodNames
    array with AScan dedup before emitting.
  - Non-visual components (Timer, DBFTable, etc.) no longer emit oFont,
    nClrPane, or lTransparent in generated code — those properties don't
    exist on non-visual controls and caused a runtime error
    (TDBFTABLE:_OFONT not found).
  - Menu bitmap positions corrected for the File menu (new items had shifted
    all positions). Exit now shows menu_exit.png, Open File shows
    menu_open.png (folder icon).
  - New Application now properly closes the previous form window
    (UI_FormHide + UI_FormClose) before destroying it, so no ghost windows
    remain on screen.
  - nAlign Center/Right mapping: the initial implementation used a direct
    cast to NSTextAlignment, which swapped Center and Right on macOS.
    Now uses conditional mapping matching createViewInParent.

2026-04-14 (Windows: TFolder page inspector view + designer drop-on-page)

  FEATURES
  - Inspector: selecting an "oFolderN:aPages[N] AS TFolderPage" entry in
    the combo now shows the page's own properties (cCaption, nPage) in a
    dedicated "Page" category instead of the folder's. cCaption is
    projected live from the folder's aTabs[N] so editing the label round-
    trips through the designer and the generated code.
  - Designer: when a palette component is pending, clicking on a TFolder
    no longer selects/drags the folder — it arcs straight into the
    rubber-band drop. The drop hit-tests the folder rect and tags the new
    control with (FPageOwner=folder, FPageIndex=active page), so the
    control becomes part of that page automatically and shows/hides with
    the tab. Codegen was already emitting OF ::oFolderN:aPages[N] for
    page-owned controls, so round-trip just works.
  - Inspector C API: new HB_FUNCs INS_SetFolderPage / INS_AddRow /
    INS_AddCategoryRow / INS_Rebuild let Harbour push synthetic rows into
    the inspector without InsPopulate overwriting them.

2026-04-14 (Windows: TLabel transparency, form-position save/restore, runtime error dialog, dropdown UX, sample improvements)

  FEATURES
  - TLabel and any TControl now expose lTransparent (default TRUE for
    TLabel, matching VCL/Delphi). Transparent statics are painted with
    NULL_BRUSH so the parent's background shows through. Inspector
    surfaces it automatically as a Yes/No dropdown.
  - When a form's nClrPane changes, every transparent / inherit-color
    child is invalidated so labels (and friends) repaint with the new
    background instead of caching the old one.
  - cFileName property in the inspector grew a "..." button that opens
    a standard Win32 file-open dialog (filter "*.dbf" by default,
    seeded with the current path). Wired into InsBtnProc + new
    InsFilePick helper.
  - User-app runtime error dialog (W32_ErrorDialog injected into every
    generated main.prg):
      * Custom dialog using the predefined "#32770" class so the
        window stops painting its own caption text as a giant label
        inside the client area.
      * EDIT control with Consolas -16, scrollable, ES_READONLY.
      * Two buttons: "Copy to clipboard" (becomes "Copied!" on click)
        and "OK". ESC closes too.
      * WS_EX_TOPMOST + SetForegroundWindow so it doesn't hide behind
        the user form.
      * LF -> CRLF normalization so AppShowError output formats with
        proper line breaks.
      * ExitProcess(1) at the end so the user-app process actually
        terminates - QUIT alone did not break the form's GetMessage
        loop, leaving zombie processes after each error.
  - REQUEST DBFCDX, DBFNTX, DBFFPT and RDDSYS injected at the top of
    every generated main.prg so TDbfTable Open() actually finds the
    DBF driver. Without this, dbUseArea threw EG_ARG/1015 on click.
  - Inspector cRDD dropdown now closes naturally when an item is
    picked. Dropped the WM_COMMAND/CBN_SELCHANGE branch in InsEditProc
    that destroyed the combo mid-drop and left the listbox hanging.
  - File > Reopen Last Project menu item, with same open icon.

  FIXES
  - Form position save/restore - "form was top-left after every open":
      * OpenProjectFile was missing the OnResize wiring, so dragging
        the design form after Open never updated FLeft/FTop and Save
        wrote stale 120/120. Wired explicitly.
      * TBSave now calls SyncDesignerToCode() before SaveActiveFormCode
        as a belt-and-braces capture of the latest position.
      * SyncDesignerToCode wraps CodeEditorSetTabText with
        lSyncingFromCode := .t./.f. so the editor change does not
        re-trigger RestoreFormFromCode (which would destroy and
        recreate every TControl, dropping in-memory state like
        TDbfTable::FRDD that was set seconds earlier).
  - Form drag flicker - WM_MOVE/WM_SIZE fired FOnResize on every pixel
    of drag, repainting the entire Scintilla tab 60 times/second.
    Added FInSizeMove flag handled by WM_ENTERSIZEMOVE/WM_EXITSIZEMOVE;
    OnResize fires once at the END of drag instead.
  - METHOD <Name>Click() handlers were emitted as plain function calls
    in the OnClick codeblock - the linker found the symbol but at
    runtime the dispatch was nonsense. Codegen now detects "METHOD
    <Name>" in the existing source and emits ::Name() (method send)
    instead of Name( Self ) (function call).
  - CLASS body did not auto-declare custom METHODs implemented below,
    so calling ::Name() raised "Message not found" at runtime. New
    ScanMethodDeclarations() walks the existing user code, picks up
    every "METHOD <Name>() CLASS <cClass>" implementation and emits a
    matching "   METHOD <Name>()" inside the CLASS body.
  - RestoreFormFromCode parser now also accepts cFileName, cRDD and
    lActive in the per-control "::oCtrl:prop := value" pass, so
    TDbfTable settings round-trip across save/load.
  - Static-text caching: TControl::SetText on a transparent label
    used to leave the old text bleeding through the new one. Hide ->
    RedrawWindow on parent rect with RDW_INVALIDATE|RDW_ERASE|RDW_
    UPDATENOW -> Show forces parent bg to repaint synchronously
    before the static draws the new text.
  - TBRun's incremental-build hash now includes hbbuilder_win.prg, so
    edits to the W32_ErrorDialog template (and any other IDE-side
    code) actually invalidate the cache and trigger a rebuild instead
    of relaunching the stale .exe.

  BACKEND (Win32)
  - TControl: new BOOL FTransparent.
  - TForm: new BOOL FInSizeMove (gates FOnResize firing during drag).
  - TLabel constructor: FTransparent = TRUE.
  - WM_CTLCOLORSTATIC: transparent branch returns NULL_BRUSH first.
  - UI_SetProp / UI_GetProp / UI_GetAllProps know "lTransparent".
  - UI_DropNonVisual: default icon table (CT_DBFTABLE -> database_
    table.png, CT_MYSQL/MARIADB/PG/SQLITE/FB/SQLSERVER/ORACLE/MONGODB
    -> database_go.png) so non-visual database components render
    with a recognisable icon when re-loaded from saved code.

  SAMPLE
  - samples/projects/dbftable/Form1.prg button handler now opens the
    DBF, reads the first field of the first record into the Edit and
    puts "<FieldName> (rec 1 of <RecCount>)" into the Label. Closes
    the table immediately. Demonstrates TDbfTable end-to-end.

---

2026-04-14 (Windows: TDbfTable backend + inspector dropdowns + global error handler + Reopen Last)

  FEATURES
  - TDbfTable non-visual component now works end-to-end on Windows:
      * FFileName[260] / FRDD[16] / FActive fields on TControl so every
        non-visual DB component has a storage slot for them.
      * UI_SetProp / UI_GetProp handle "cFileName", "cRDD", "lActive".
      * UI_GetAllProps adds a case CT_DBFTABLE that exposes the three
        under a new "Data" category so they show up in the inspector.
      * UI_DropNonVisual resolves a default icon by CT_ when the caller
        does not pass one: CT_DBFTABLE -> database_table.png,
        CT_MYSQL/MARIADB/POSTGRESQL/SQLITE/FIREBIRD/SQLSERVER/ORACLE/
        MONGODB -> database_go.png (absolute paths to the repo's
        resources/icons/ folder).
  - Inspector dropdowns extended to two new modes:
      * ENUMDEF now carries a bIsString flag. When TRUE the dropdown
        stores the chosen string verbatim (not an index), matching by
        strcmp on initial selection. cRDD uses this: "DBFCDX" /
        "DBFNTX" / "DBFFPT".
      * Any row whose cType is 'L' (PT_LOGICAL) automatically gets a
        synthetic Yes/No combobox even without a named enum entry.
        Stored value is written back as ".T." / ".F." so the rest of
        the codegen does not change.
  - File > "Reopen &Last Project" menuitem. Opens the most recent
    project from a persistent [Recent] section in hbbuilder.ini, up to
    MAX_RECENT=8 entries, newest-first, deduped on every open. Uses the
    same menu_open.png bitmap as Open... - and the File menu bitmap at
    positions 5 (Save) / 6 (Save As) / 8 (Exit) is adjusted for the new
    menu item so every row still shows its icon.
  - Global ErrorBlock installed in Main() before any UI is created.
    Unhandled runtime errors now surface a W32_BuildErrorDialog showing
    class / subsystem / GenCode / SubCode / description / operation /
    args / full call stack (via ProcName + ProcLine + ProcFile), then
    propagate Break so the IDE unwinds to its outer message loop
    instead of dying silently. Also appends to
    c:\HarbourBuilder\error_trace.log for later inspection. This
    immediately surfaced a BASE/1066 in RegenerateFormCode where
    UI_GetProp(hCtrl, "lActive") returned NIL for non-visual components
    that do not implement it - guarded with a ValType()=="L" check.
  - New sample samples/projects/dbftable/ demonstrating the flow: a
    TLabel + TEdit + TButton + non-visual oDbfTable1 with cFileName
    and cRDD set. README explains what to try.

  FIXES
  - RegenerateFormCode line 855: UI_GetProp(hCtrl, "lActive") returning
    NIL on a backend that did not recognize the property crashed with
    "Argument error conditional" inside every form designer click.
    Defensive guard: only proceed when ValType() == "L". Same pattern
    for "cRDD" -> only emit the assignment when ValType() == "C".
  - OpenProjectFile refactor: the bulk of TBOpen is now a shared helper
    that both TBOpen (after the file dialog) and ReopenLastProject /
    future recent-list menu items can reuse without duplicating the
    "destroy current forms, clear tabs, read prg files, rewire
    callbacks" logic.
  - Parser of "COMPONENT ::oName TYPE ... OF Self" now strips a
    trailing ':' from the captured cName so phantom controls do not
    sneak in when the saved code has ':'.

  BACKEND (Win32)
  - TForm::FAppTitle and UI_GetAllProps "cAppTitle" entry (already
    shipped) are joined now by CT_DBFTABLE handling: three properties
    + one icon mapping + three getter/setter branches.

2026-04-14 (Windows catches up with macOS: AppTitle property + full CT_* name resolver)

  FEATURES
  - NEW cAppTitle property on TForm. Visible in the inspector under a
    new "Application" category. The name the user types becomes the
    .exe file name at build time, so what they ship matches what they
    named. Empty falls back to the historical "UserApp.exe".
    Persisted in the generated form code as ::AppTitle := "...", and
    the form loader parses it back into the live form.
    (Matches macOS 35060e9 where the same property drives the app
    menu name and the .app bundle.)

  FIXES
  - ComponentTypeFromName() in hbbuilder_win.prg was missing 40+ entries
    beyond CT_HTTPCLIENT: AI (46-52), threading (63-70), internet
    (74-78), data-aware (79-86), ERP/printing/connectivity (90-120),
    Git (121-130). Replaced the hand-written do case list with a
    42-entry aMap that mirrors macOS 8ca8d24. Forms saved with the
    symbolic CT_* names now load correctly on Windows instead of
    silently dropping to type 0.
  - Parser of "COMPONENT ::oName TYPE ... OF Self" now strips a
    trailing ':' from the captured name - previously left it attached
    to cName, producing phantom controls.

  BACKEND (Win32)
  - TForm grew a char FAppTitle[128] (hbide.h). Initialized empty in
    TForm constructor. UI_SetProp/UI_GetProp route "cAppTitle" to it
    (hbbridge.cpp). UI_GetAllProps exposes it so the Win32 inspector
    shows it under the "Application" category.

2026-04-14 (Android Setup Wizard + prebuilt Harbour-for-Android shipped in repo)

  FEATURES
  - NEW menu Run > "Android Setup Wizard..." next to Run on Android.
    Checks 9 toolchain components (NDK r26d, SDK platform 34,
    build-tools 34, platform-tools, emulator, JDK 17, Git Bash,
    Harbour-for-Android libs, AVD HarbourBuilderAVD) and reports each
    as OK / MISSING. If anything is missing and Git Bash is present,
    offers to run the full installer in a dedicated terminal window.
  - NEW source/backends/android/setup-android-toolchain.sh - one
    script that downloads and installs every external component a
    fresh machine needs, into fixed paths under C:\. Idempotent:
    detects what is already in place and skips it.
      * JDK 17 Temurin (Adoptium)                 ~175 MB
      * Android NDK r26d (dl.google.com)          ~1.5 GB
      * SDK cmdline-tools (dl.google.com)         ~100 MB
      * SDK packages via sdkmanager (platform 34, build-tools 34,
        platform-tools, emulator, system-image android-34 x86_64)  ~1.2 GB
      * AVD HarbourBuilderAVD (Pixel 5) via avdmanager
      * Harbour-for-Android libs extracted from releases/ (shipped
        in the repo, 3.6 MB prebuilt)
    Uses curl for downloads and PowerShell Expand-Archive for zips.
    Auto-applies the NDK ar/ranlib/strip tweak that Harbour mk files
    need. Pipes 'yes' into sdkmanager --licenses so the installer
    doesn't block on license prompts.
  - NEW releases/harbour-android-arm64-v8a.zip (3.6 MB) - 30 static
    .a libraries (libhbvm, libhbrtl, libgttrm, rddntx, ...) plus 72
    headers, all cross-compiled from official harbour/core 3.2.0dev
    r2502031126 with NDK Clang for aarch64-linux-android24. Shipping
    the prebuilt means a fresh clone skips the 5-10 minute
    bootstrap-harbour.sh step entirely - the wizard just extracts it.
  - NEW source/backends/android/bootstrap-harbour.sh - the recipe
    that produced the shipped zip, versioned for users who want to
    track upstream Harbour changes or target other ABIs.
  - NEW source/backends/android/SETUP.md - end-to-end manual setup
    guide (toolchain tables, NDK tweak, AVD creation, bootstrap,
    validation, troubleshooting) for users who prefer to install by
    hand or can't use the Wizard yet.
  - NEW source/backends/android/run-on-emulator.sh - standalone AVD
    bootstrap companion to the newer install-and-run.sh (kept for
    direct-shell usage).
  - Run > Run on Android and Run > Android Setup Wizard land in the
    same submenu so the flow is obvious: Wizard once, then Run on
    Android as many times as needed.

  OUT OF SCOPE (roadmap)
  - Inline download progress inside the IDE dialog (today the
    installer shell window shows curl/sdkmanager output live,
    which is honest and easy to follow).
  - macOS and Linux wizard port (same script, different URLs/paths
    and PowerShell replaced with unzip).
  - Multi-ABI prebuilt zips (x86_64, armeabi-v7a).

2026-04-14 (Android iteration 1b + 1c: form designer -> APK with working click handlers, colors and fonts)

  FEATURES
  - Run > Run on Android... now drops the user's IDE form straight
    onto the emulator. End-to-end flow: drop controls in the designer,
    write a METHOD Button1Click() CLASS TForm1 handler with the usual
    ::oLabel1:Text := "..." + ::oEdit1:Text + "..." style, hit the
    menu. The IDE regenerates _generated.prg, builds a signed APK,
    boots HarbourBuilderAVD if needed, installs, launches and tails
    logcat in a dedicated terminal. Validated live on Pixel 5
    (Android 14) 2026-04-14.
  - Code generator (GenerateAndroidPRG in hbbuilder_win.prg) walks the
    live oDesignForm, emits UI_FormNew + per-control UI_LabelNew /
    UI_EditNew / UI_ButtonNew with exact pixel coordinates, wires
    UI_OnClick for buttons whose handler exists in the form code.
    Control handles are emitted as module-scope STATICs so the
    separate handler FUNCTIONs can see them.
  - Handler translator: extracts METHOD <Name>Click() bodies from the
    user's form prg, rewrites them as plain FUNCTIONs and translates
    ::oXxx:Text getters/setters into UI_GetText / UI_SetText calls
    against the backend handles. Missing handlers fall back to empty
    stubs so the Android linker never reports an unresolved symbol.
  - Colors and fonts carried over from the designer:
      * UI_SetFormColor( nColor )            - Form.Color / nClrPane
      * UI_SetCtrlColor( hCtrl, nColor )     - per-control nClrPane
      * UI_SetCtrlFont ( hCtrl, cFace, nSp ) - parses "Segoe UI,12"
    Win32 COLORREF (0x00BBGGRR) is byte-swapped to Android ARGB
    (0xFFRRGGBB) in android_core.c via a bgr_to_argb helper. Font
    family mapping: mono/courier/consolas -> Typeface.MONOSPACE,
    serif/times/georgia -> Typeface.SERIF, anything else falls back
    to Typeface.DEFAULT (Roboto). Size passed as SP.
  - Auto-emulator boot moved into install-and-run.sh. The IDE spawns
    the script in its own terminal window (title "HarbourBuilder
    Android") and returns control immediately. The script does
    adb start-server, launches HarbourBuilderAVD if nothing is
    connected, polls sys.boot_completed, installs the APK, starts the
    activity and tails logcat live. A trap EXIT + "Press enter to
    close" keeps the window open on failure so errors are readable.
  - samples/projects/android/ - ready-to-open Label+Edit+Button sample
    that exercises the whole path, plus README.md with prerequisites.

  FIXES
  - W32_ShellExec already prefixes 'cmd /c' internally; TBRunAndroid
    stopped adding another cmd /c on top. Without that fix the triple
    'cmd /c cmd /c "..."' quoting collapsed and the build silently
    no-op'd, installing a stale APK every time.
  - cmd.exe /c rule 2 ("strip first and last quote") was eating a
    real quote from the bash path. Wrapped the whole command in an
    outer pair of double-quotes so rule 2 has something to strip.
  - Generated PRG used LOCAL hXxx in Main(), invisible to the handler
    FUNCTIONs. Switched to module-scope STATICs; first button tap no
    longer crashes with "variable does not exist".
  - MainActivity.java method name setText(int,String) collided with
    Context.setText(int resId) which is final; renamed to setCtrlText
    / getCtrlText and updated JNI lookups.
  - build-apk-gui.sh d8/apksigner calls reference the .bat wrappers
    (Windows build-tools don't install bare 'd8'); packaging uses
    jar.exe uf + zipalign.exe instead of 'zip' (not in Git Bash PATH).
  - build-apk-gui.log moved out of /c/HarbourAndroid/apk-gui/ because
    build-apk-gui.sh rm -rf's that directory at startup, taking the
    log with it. Now at /c/HarbourAndroid/build-apk-gui.log, visible
    to the IDE build-error dialog.
  - .gitignore un-ignores source/backends/**/*.c (the top-level
    'backends/' negation didn't match the nested path).

  DEBUG INSTRUMENTATION
  - AndroidTrace() appends timestamped entries to
    C:\HarbourBuilder\android_trace.log at every step of TBRunAndroid
    and GenerateAndroidPRG (paths, sizes, control enumeration, build
    cmd, launch cmd, return codes).

  ROADMAP (not yet)
  - ComboBox, CheckBox, RadioButton, ListView, DatePicker bindings in
    android_core.c / MainActivity.java.
  - Embedded logcat panel inside the IDE (today it streams in a
    separate cmd window).
  - Device picker (emulator / USB / Wi-Fi ADB).
  - Keystore manager + AAB export for Play Store.
  - Android toolchain auto-installer wizard (NDK, SDK, JDK, AVD) for
    Windows, macOS, Linux.
  - iOS backend (ios_core.m via UIKit) mirroring the Cocoa one.

2026-04-13 (Android target - iteration 1: GUI backend, end-to-end APK pipeline from the IDE)

  FEATURES
  - NEW Android target. Menu Run > "Run on Android..." on the Windows
    IDE drives the full pipeline: saves the current Project1.prg, runs
    bash build-apk.sh (harbour.exe -> NDK clang -> aapt2 -> javac -> d8 ->
    zipalign -> apksigner), and launches the signed APK on the
    HarbourBuilderAVD emulator. Validated end-to-end on Pixel 5 /
    Android 14 with a 509 KB signed APK.
  - NEW source/backends/android/ — 4th native GUI backend:
      * android_core.c — JNI bridge. HB_FUNCs UI_FormNew, UI_LabelNew,
        UI_ButtonNew, UI_EditNew, UI_SetText, UI_GetText, UI_OnClick,
        UI_FormRun (no-op: Activity owns the loop), plus the
        UI_SetCtrlOwner / UI_GetCtrlPage / UI_TabControlNew page-owner
        stubs so classes.prg links.
      * java/com/harbour/builder/MainActivity.java — programmatic
        FrameLayout host (no XML layout). Exposes createForm /
        createLabel / createButton / createEdit / setText / getText /
        nativeOnClick to JNI. HashMap<Integer,View> keyed by the
        numeric control id returned from the UI_*New calls.
      * build-apk-gui.sh — parallel GUI pipeline that stages sources
        from the repo, compiles android_core.c alongside the user's
        PRG, links libapp.so, and signs harbour-gui.apk.
      * hello_gui.prg — demo calling UI_FormNew + UI_LabelNew +
        UI_EditNew + UI_ButtonNew + UI_OnClick end-to-end.
      * AndroidManifest.xml, res/values/strings.xml.
  - Density-aware layout: MainActivity multiplies form-designer pixels
    by DisplayMetrics.density so a 100-px button looks consistent on
    mdpi, hdpi, xxhdpi screens.
  - Click dispatch: Java onClick -> nativeOnClick(controlId) -> C
    evaluates the Harbour codeblock registered with UI_OnClick(id,block).
  - Event loop is inverted vs desktop: UI_FormRun() is a no-op; the
    Android Activity owns the message pump and widgets live inside its
    lifecycle.

  WIN32 LINK FIXES
  - Added TPageControl page-ownership stubs to source/cpp/hbbridge.cpp
    (UI_SetCtrlOwner, UI_GetCtrlOwner, UI_GetCtrlPage,
    UI_SetPendingPageOwner, UI_TabControlNew) — no-ops for now so the
    Win32 IDE links. Real TPageControl support on Win32 will come when
    the form designer gains a Pages tab.
  - Guarded the Python #pragma BEGINDUMP block in source/core/classes.prg
    with #if defined(HB_OS_WIN): Windows gets no-op stubs for PY_Start,
    PY_Exec, PY_Eval, PY_SetVar, PY_GetVar, PY_GetOutput, PY_LastError,
    PY_IsAvailable, PY_Stop; macOS/Linux keep the real dlopen backend.
    Unblocks the bcc32 build on Windows (dlfcn.h isn't available and
    C99 mid-block decls were rejected).

  DOCS
  - README.md: new "NEW - Now going Mobile" section with Android/iOS
    badges, 5-backend architecture diagram, iteration 1 checklist, and
    iOS teaser. Platform badge extended to include Android + iOS.
  - docs/index.html: new #mobile section with two side-by-side cards
    (Android available now / iOS coming soon) using inline SVG logos,

2026-04-13 (macOS: real in-process Python via dlopen, Python sample, codegen fixes)

  FEATURES
  - TPython now executes code IN-PROCESS via a dlopen'd libpython.
    Neither the IDE nor compiled apps link libpython statically: the
    first TPython:Start() tries common paths (Homebrew, system
    frameworks, libpython3.X.dylib); if none is found, cLastError
    explains why and the program keeps running. Implemented in a
    `#pragma BEGINDUMP` block inside classes.prg — HB_FUNCs:
    PY_Start / PY_Stop / PY_Exec / PY_Eval / PY_SetVar / PY_GetVar /
    PY_GetOutput / PY_LastError / PY_IsAvailable.
  - sys.stdout and sys.stderr are redirected to an in-memory StringIO
    that PY_GetOutput reads after each call and feeds back to the
    form via the OnOutput event.
  - TPython overrides Start/Stop/Exec/Eval/SetVar/GetVar to call the
    backend and fire OnReady / OnError / OnOutput.
  - TInteropRuntime now inherits from TControl so runtime components
    get :oFont, :Left, :Top, :Color, etc. (runtime assignments are
    no-ops; design-time goes through the real HBControl handle).
  - samples/projects/python rewritten as a real beginner demo: a
    sample chooser ComboBox, an editable script Memo, Run / Eval /
    Clear buttons, and an output Memo.

  FIXES
  - COMBOBOX xcommand now delegates to a TComboBox:FillItems() method
    that guards against nil aItems (avoids the "ValType() with 0 args"
    expansion error when the ITEMS clause is absent).
  - ComboBox items survive IDE save: codegen reads them via
    UI_ComboGetCount / UI_ComboGetItem and emits ITEMS { "a","b" };
    parser picks them up and calls UI_ComboAddItem.
  - Multi-line Harbour statements (with `;` line continuations) are
    joined before tokenizing in RestoreFormFromCode so clauses
    spanning lines parse correctly.
  - Memo text round-trip: CT_MEMO createViewInParent applies FText to
    the new NSTextView, UI_SetProp("cText") updates the NSTextView
    when FView exists, codegen emits `::oMemo:Text := "..."` and the
    parser rebuilds the literal from `"..." + Chr(N) + "..."` chains.
  - Second-pass property parser is restricted to the CreateForm body
    so assignments inside user methods (e.g. `::oMemo:Text := cCode`
    inside LoadSample) no longer overwrite design-time values.
  - Codegen preserves any user-added METHOD declaration in the CLASS
    block and any `::oCtrl:xxx := ...` line from the CreateForm body
    that the built-in emitter doesn't already produce (OnClick
    codeblocks, TPython :cRuntimePath / :OnReady / :OnOutput, etc.).
  - Form :Position round-trips: codegen emits `::Position := N`;
    parser detects `::Position := N`; inspector dropdown gained the
    missing `poDefault` entry so indices align with hbbuilder.ch.
  - Form centering computed from [[NSScreen mainScreen] visibleFrame]
    instead of [NSWindow center] so the window sits exactly in the
    middle of the usable screen area.

  FILES
  - source/core/classes.prg: Python BEGINDUMP backend, TPython method
    overrides, TInteropRuntime inherits TControl, TComboBox:FillItems.
  - source/backends/cocoa/cocoa_core.m: geometric center helper, Memo
    applies FText on view creation + live update on setProp, nPosition
    enum has poDefault.
  - source/hbbuilder_macos.prg: codegen for ComboBox ITEMS and Memo
    Text and ::Position, parser for ::Text / ::Position / ComboBox
    ITEMS, line-continuation join, CreateForm-scoped property pass,
    preserved METHOD declarations and user-written assignments.
  - include/hbbuilder.ch: COMBOBOX xcommand uses :FillItems().
  - samples/projects/python: real beginner sample.

2026-04-13 (macOS: Connectivity components — TPython and 8 siblings via TInteropRuntime)

  FEATURES
  - New class hierarchy for the Connectivity palette tab:
    - TInteropRuntime (base) with shared properties: cRuntimePath,
      cScript, cScriptFile, lAutoStart, aModules, cLastResult,

    palette position, not by ctrlType). palBtnClicked, UI_DropNonVisual

    save/load: codegen appends `@ L,T` to the trailing comment on the

    after UI_DropNonVisual.

    names survive reopen.

  - palBtnClicked non-visual path now calls KeepAlive(ctrl); otherwise
    the freshly created control was not in s_allControls and the
    stricter GetCtrlRaw validator returned nil, breaking the inspector
    combo, drag, and triggering "Argument error: +" in codegen.
  - IDE-wide ErrorBlock installed at Main() that writes error +
    call-stack to /tmp/hb_ide.err (returns NIL so Harbour handles the
    default dialog without poisoning downstream values).
  - RegenerateFormCode cParent helper guards against UI_GetProp
    returning nil so "+ NIL" is avoided for stale owner handles.
  - TFolder-style `OF ::oFolder:aPages[n]` parser skipped auto-page
    TPanels in codegen (flagged FAutoPage) so they are re-created by
    the aTabs setter instead of duplicated.

  NEW SAMPLE

    that shows a TPython component driven from the form (script memo,

  FILES

    TNode, TRust, TJava, TDotNet, TLua, TRuby; HB_CreateComponent
    dispatch for types 112..120.

  - source/hbbuilder_macos.prg: ErrorBlock + IdeDumpError + Var2Char;
    guarded cParent helper in RegenerateFormCode; `@ L,T` emission on
    COMPONENT lines; parser restores non-visual designer position.
  - samples/projects/python: new sample.

2026-04-13 (macOS: TTreeView class and hierarchical aItems editor)

  FEATURES
  - TTreeView class with `aItems` property edited from the inspector via
    the same multi-line list dialog used for TBrowse/TFolder.
    - Indentation defines hierarchy: 2 leading spaces = 1 tree level.
        Root1
          Child1
          Child2
            Grandchild
        Root2

  FIXES

    whitespace when saving, so indentation survives the round-trip
    designer <-> dialog. Trailing whitespace is still stripped; fully
    blank lines are dropped.
  - Codegen for TREEVIEW emits each item with `RTrim(...)` instead of
    `AllTrim(...)` so the run-time project keeps the hierarchy.

2026-04-13 (macOS: TFolder + TFolderPage, FiveWin-style FOLDER ... PROMPTS syntax)

  REFACTOR
  - Renamed TTabControl -> TFolder and adopted FiveWin-style syntax:
      @ T, L FOLDER ::oFolder1 OF Self SIZE W, H PROMPTS "A", "B"
      @ T, L BUTTON ::oBtn1 PROMPT "..." OF ::oFolder1:aPages[1] SIZE w, h
  - New TFolderPage class: lightweight container for a tab page. Its
    `:hCpp` ACCESS signals a pending page-owner to the backend and returns
    the host form's handle, so controls read naturally as children of the
    page while the backend stays flat (ownership applied in addChild).
  - `aPages` array (one TFolderPage per tab) replaces the separate
    `:oOwner` / `:nPage` metadata in generated code.
  - Palette entry: TFolder (tooltip + class), default name "Folder1".
  - hbbuilder.ch: `#xcommand @ T,L FOLDER ... OF ... SIZE ... PROMPTS ...`.

  FEATURES
  - Added TTabControl HB_FUNC `UI_SetPendingPageOwner(hFolder, nPage)`:
    queued by TFolderPage:hCpp and consumed by the next addChild so the
    newly added control inherits the page ownership transparently.
  - Codegen: emits `FOLDER ... PROMPTS ...` and for owned controls the
    parent expression becomes `::oFolder:aPages[ n+1 ]`.
  - Parser: recognizes `FOLDER ... PROMPTS ...` lines and detects
    `OF ::oFolder:aPages[ n ]` in control creation lines to restore
    ownership via `UI_SetCtrlOwner`.

  FILES
  - source/core/classes.prg: TFolderPage, TFolder (aPages, aPrompts,
    New, SetPrompts); TControl gained `oOwner`/`nPage` ASSIGN helpers.
  - include/hbbuilder.ch: FOLDER xcommand with PROMPTS.
  - source/backends/cocoa/cocoa_core.m: UI_SetPendingPageOwner, pending
    owner applied in addChild, palette entry renamed to TFolder.
  - source/hbbuilder_macos.prg: codegen emits FOLDER/PROMPTS + parent
    expression `::oFolder:aPages[n]`; parser recognizes both the new
    command and the `:aPages[n]` clause; old `oOwner`/`nPage` emission
    removed; default name generator renamed TabView -> Folder.

2026-04-13 (macOS: TTabControl -> TPageControl with auto-page TPanels and ownership)

  FEATURES
  - TTabControl now behaves like a TPageControl (C++Builder style):
    - New `aTabs` property on TTabControl, edited via the same multi-line
      string list dialog used for TBrowse `aHeaders`/`aColumns`.
    - Auto-creates one TPanel per tab (FAutoPage flag, name `<name>_Page<i>`)
      as the page container; removed/recreated when `aTabs` changes.
    - Click on the tab bar in design mode switches the active page AND
      still lets you select/drag the control.
    - Auto-page panels are selectable (as drop target) but not movable or
      resizable — geometry is controlled by the owning TPageControl.
    - Dropping a control inside the TPageControl content area, or while an
      auto-page is selected, assigns ownership (FOwnerCtrl, FOwnerPage).
      The control is shown only when its page is active; hidden otherwise.
    - Moving a TPageControl translates all its owned controls with it.
    - Codegen: emits `@ T,L TABCONTROL ::oName OF Self SIZE W,H TABS "A","B"`
      plus `::oCtrl:oOwner := ::oPC` / `::oCtrl:nPage := n` for owned
      controls. Parser regenerates ownership via UI_SetCtrlOwner.
    - Auto-page TPanels are skipped in codegen — rebuilt automatically by
      the `aTabs` setter.
  - UI_SetCtrlOwner / UI_GetCtrlOwner / UI_GetCtrlPage / UI_IsAutoPage
    HB_FUNCs exposed to Harbour.

  FIXES
  - GetCtrlRaw now validates handles against s_allControls before the
    __bridge cast; prevents `objc_retain` crash on stale handles returned
    by the inspector combo map after a form rebuild.
  - SyncDesignerToCode guards against re-entry via lSyncingFromCode around
    CodeEditorSetTabText.
  - OnEditorTextChange also bails out when the debounced text equals the
    last code we regenerated, so the 500ms text-change timer no longer
    tears down child controls (and thus no longer deselects the user's
    current selection).
  - Find/Replace panel: moved the Close button 10px right so it no longer
    overlaps Replace All; renamed "Replace All" to "Rep. All" so the title
    fits; Replace and Rep. All are hidden in Find-only mode.
  - NSTabView design-time delegate uses a `__weak` back-reference to the
    owner so tab change events on a freed control no longer crash.
  - Array editor sheet: explicit initialFirstResponder + makeFirstResponder
    + activateIgnoringOtherApps so typing is always routed to the text view.

  FILES
  - source/backends/cocoa/cocoa_core.m: TPageControl ownership plumbing
    (FOwnerCtrl, FOwnerPage, FAutoPage, FPendingOwner), HBTabDelegate,
    UI_TabControlNew, UI_SetCtrlOwner / UI_GetCtrlOwner / UI_GetCtrlPage /
    UI_IsAutoPage, aTabs live update with auto-panel create/remove,
    overlay acceptsFirstMouse, GetCtrlRaw validation.
  - source/backends/cocoa/cocoa_inspector.m: focus fixes for the array
    editor sheet.
  - source/hbbuilder_macos.prg: TABCONTROL codegen + parser, oOwner/nPage
    codegen + parser, OnPropChanged refresh combo, SyncDesignerToCode
    re-entry guard, OnEditorTextChange no-op on identical code.
