2026-04-13 (Linux: form loading, runtime control creation, label auto-size,
            multi-select rubber-band, palette icons)

  FIXES
  - Loading a project's form from disk showed the form empty (no colour,
    no controls). Root causes:
      * UI_*New() on GTK3 only stored the HBControl; the real GTK widgets
        were created later inside HBForm_Show. After Show, runtime-added
        children (sync from editor, palette drop) had no widget. Now
        HBControl_AddChild auto-calls HBControl_CreateWidget when the
        parent form is already shown (FFixed exists).
      * HBForm_CreateControlOfType no longer creates the widget a second
        time — AddChild handles it; it only calls gtk_widget_show_all.
      * CodeEditor's CE_SwitchTab (hit by CodeEditorSelectTab at the end
        of TBOpen) called SCI_SETTEXT without setting bSettingText, so
        Scintilla queued a debounced SCN_MODIFIED. 500 ms later the
        editor→designer sync fired, ran UI_FormClearChildren and a
        second RestoreFormFromCode, invalidating the inspector combo
        map pointers. CE_SwitchTab now wraps the text update with
        bSettingText=1.
      * OnEditorTextChange additionally short-circuits when the editor
        text hasn't actually changed (compared against aForms[i][3]),
        so any stray debounced notification can't destroy live
        HBControls.
  - Clicking a control on a loaded form selected it on mouse-down but
    lost the selection on mouse-up. The combo-change handler
    (OnComboSelect → UI_FormSelectCtrl) re-entered HBForm_SelectControl
    which cleared and re-added the control, unnecessarily, and on the
    release path the stale combo map was triggering extra selection
    resets. UI_FormSelectCtrl now short-circuits when the target is
    already selected, which also lets multi-selection survive combo
    echoes.
  - TLabel auto-grows to fit its text when the stored SIZE is too
    narrow for the current font (typical when a macOS font falls back
    on Linux). HBControl_ApplyFont measures the text with Pango for
    CT_LABEL and expands FWidth/FHeight before set_size_request.
  - Palette icons in the Standard tab were keyed by nControlType, but
    resources/palette.bmp is laid out sequentially following the
    AddComp() order across tabs (the same convention macOS already
    used). UI_PaletteLoadImages on GTK3 now uses imgBase+btnIdx,
    and Standard tab reorders Memo/Button to match. The non-visual
    control-type icon cache is populated from the correct slice.
  - Form background colour, applied via a per-form GtkCssProvider,
    could be overridden by the global dark-mode provider (same
    selector, priority APPLICATION+1). Forms whose FClrPane was set
    explicitly (via UI_SetProp / project load / Inspector) now install
    their CSS with PRIORITY_USER and skip the install for default/IDE
    forms, so dark mode still paints those.

  FEATURES
  - Rubber-band multi-selection on the designer. Pressing on empty
    form area starts a dotted selection rectangle (on_overlay_draw
    already drew it when FRubberBand was set, but it was only used
    for palette drops). Release selects every control intersecting
    the rectangle.

2026-04-12 (macOS: runtime form position matches design, test sample)

  FIXES
  - Runtime form window appeared ~30px above its design-time position on
    macOS. POS_DESIGNED placement used FHeight (content-only height) when
    flipping Y for setFrameOrigin, which expects the full frame height
    (incl. title bar). Now reads the window's actual frame height. Same
    fix applied to UI_FormSetPos.

  SAMPLES
  - Added samples/projects/test (Project1.hbp/prg + Form1.prg), a small
    macOS sample with a label, edit and button wired to hb_memowrit.

2026-04-12 (macOS: designer two-way sync on project load, live Edit text)

  FIXES
  - Form designer: opening an existing project no longer made controls
    disappear after a brief flash. RestoreFormFromCode only repopulated
    FChildren via UI_*New() which on macOS only call addChild (no NSView
    creation). Added UI_FormRebuildChildren in cocoa_core.m, invoked from
    SyncDesignerFromCode, to recreate NSViews after re-parse.
  - Form background colour disappeared on re-parse because
    UI_FormClearChildren was removing the HBDotGridView (which renders
    nClrPane in design mode). It now preserves the dot grid alongside
    the overlay view.
  - Re-entry path in createWindowWithRunLoop (cocoa_core.m) now re-adds
    dot grid and overlay in design mode after wiping subviews, so a
    second Show/Activate keeps the designer chrome.
  - Moving/resizing the designer window didn't update code or inspector
    for forms loaded from a project file — the project-load loop wired
    OnSelChange and OnComponentDrop but skipped OnResize. It now calls
    WireDesignForm() so the two-way sync works consistently.
  - TEdit/TMemo :Text returned the cached FText buffer instead of the
    live value typed by the user. UI_GetProp("cText") now reads
    stringValue from NSTextField (or string from NSTextView) for
    CT_EDIT and CT_MEMO before returning, matching Win32 semantics.

2026-04-12 (macOS: standard dialog components, autocomplete popup, palette icons)

  FEATURES
  - TOpenDialog / TSaveDialog / TFontDialog / TColorDialog now work on
    macOS. New resources/stddlgs_mac.mm implements MAC_ExecOpenDialog
    (NSOpenPanel), MAC_ExecSaveDialog (NSSavePanel), MAC_ExecFontDialog
    (NSFontPanel with custom OK/Cancel accessory view and colour via
    changeAttributes:), MAC_ExecColorDialog (NSColorPanel with
    OK/Cancel accessory). Colours are exchanged in Win32-style BGR so
    the same user code works across platforms.
  - source/core/classes.prg: Execute() methods gain a __PLATFORM__DARWIN
    branch alongside the existing __PLATFORM__WINDOWS one.
  - source/hbbuilder_macos.prg: TBRun and DBGRun copy stddlgs_mac.mm
    into the build dir, compile it with clang++ -fobjc-arc, and link
    stddlgs_mac.o into the user binary (and DebugApp).
  - build_mac.sh: new [3c/4] step compiles stddlgs_mac.o, linker picks
    it up so HB_FUN_MAC_EXEC* symbols resolve in the IDE itself;
    stddlgs_mac.mm is bundled into .app/Contents/Resources/ for the
    user-project build path.

  FIXES
  - Autocomplete popup no longer closes when the debounced form-sync
    timer fires. cocoa_editor.mm fireTextChange: now checks
    SCI_AUTOCACTIVE and reschedules itself 300 ms later instead of
    invoking the Harbour text-change callback (which rewrites the
    buffer and cancels the active list). Matches the Win32 fix.
  - Component palette icons were misaligned: palette.bmp is laid out
    sequentially in AddComp order, but cocoa_core.m PalShowTab indexed
    it as (nControlType - 1). Since nControlType values are not
    contiguous (1,2,3,4,8,…), CheckBox (nType=4) displayed the Memo
    cell, RadioButton (nType=8) displayed a wrong icon, etc. Switched
    to imgBase + i indexing (same scheme as Win32 tcontrols.cpp).
  - hbbuilder_macos.prg Standard palette tab: Memo and Button were
    swapped relative to Windows, so once sequential indexing was in
    place the first cells drifted. Reordered to match palette.bmp.
  - Autocomplete: typing `oForm:oOpenDialog1:` (or any other dialog
    component) produced no dropdown. cocoa_editor.mm s_classMembers
    gains TOpenDialog / TSaveDialog / TFontDialog / TColorDialog /
    TFindDialog / TReplaceDialog entries, and the Hungarian-prefix
    resolver s_nameMap recognises OpenDialog/SaveDialog/FontDialog/
    ColorDialog/FindDialog/ReplaceDialog so Strategy 4 maps the var
    name to its class.

2026-04-12 (Windows: standard dialog components + autocomplete + palette fixes)

  FEATURES
  - Standard dialog components usable from user projects: TOpenDialog,
    TSaveDialog, TFontDialog, TColorDialog, TFindDialog, TReplaceDialog
    added to source/core/classes.prg. Each exposes DATAs (cFileName,
    cFilter, cInitialDir, cTitle, cDefaultExt, nOptions / cFontName,
    nSize, nColor, nStyle / nColor / cFindText, cReplaceText, bOnFind,
    bOnReplace) and an Execute() method.
  - HB_CreateComponent() in classes.prg maps CT_OPENDIALOG..CT_REPLACEDIALOG
    to their classes so `COMPONENT ::oOpenDialog1 TYPE CT_OPENDIALOG`
    produces a live object at runtime.
  - resources/stddlgs.c: Win32 backends (W32_ExecOpenDialog /
    W32_ExecSaveDialog / W32_ExecFontDialog / W32_ExecColorDialog)
    using GetOpenFileNameA / GetSaveFileNameA / ChooseFontA /
    ChooseColorA with a Delphi-style "A (*.a)|*.a|B|*.b" filter parser
    that produces the double-NUL format Win32 expects.
  - Project build flow copies resources/stddlgs.c into the build dir,
    compiles it for MSVC/MinGW/BCC, and links stddlgs.obj/.o alongside
    main + classes. TFindDialog/TReplaceDialog:Execute() currently
    invoke their on* callbacks (no modeless UI yet).
  - samples/projects/opendialog added — minimal project showing
    `if ::oOpenDialog1:Execute(); MsgInfo( ::oOpenDialog1:cFileName )`.

  FIXES
  - Code-editor autocomplete (SCN_CHARADDED, ':'):
    * SCI_AUTOCSETORDER was dispatched as message 2235 instead of 2660,
      leaving Scintilla in SC_ORDER_PRESORTED and running a binary
      search on an unsorted list — entries like user DATAs appended to
      the end of the list silently disappeared from the dropdown. Fixed
      to 2660 so SC_ORDER_PERFORMSORT actually takes effect.
    * CE_CollectUserData / CE_FindClassMembers / CE_ResolveVarClass
      used hardcoded Scintilla message IDs 2009/2094/2095 that map to
      SCI_GETLENGTH/SCI_GETCOLUMN/SCI_SETHSCROLLBAR, not the line
      helpers intended. Replaced with the SCI_GETLINECOUNT (2154) /
      SCI_LINELENGTH (2350) / SCI_GETLINE (2153) constants already
      declared in the file — the class-member scan now actually reads
      lines, so `oForm:` dropdown finally picks up user DATAs.
    * CE_FindClassMembers: when cls resolves to "TForm", substitute
      the user's subclass (any `CLASS X FROM TForm` found in any tab)
      so its DATAs are collected via CE_CollectUserData. Without this
      Strategy 2 (`oForm := TForm():New()`) preempted the naming-
      convention lookup and only standard TForm members showed.
    * WM_TIMER debounced text-change callback (500ms) closed the active
      autocomplete popup on its way to re-parsing the form. It now
      checks SCI_AUTOCACTIVE and reschedules itself (300ms) instead of
      running while the dropdown is visible.
  - Standard dialog class members added to s_classMembers so
    `oForm:oOpenDialog1:` shows cFileName/cFilter/Execute()/... in the
    dropdown (previously "(null)" → no popup).
  - RegenerateFormCode: skip emitting :oFont and :nClrPane for
    IsNonVisual(nType) controls. Non-visual components (TOpenDialog
    etc.) have no oFont DATA, so the generated code was crashing with
    "No exported variable OFONT" the moment a form with an OpenDialog
    was run.
  - resources/palette.bmp: first-tab cells 3..8 were misaligned vs.
    source PNGs (TMemo showed a checkbox, TRadioButton showed a panel,
    TComboBox showed a radio button, TGroupBox showed a memo). Cells
    regenerated from resources/lazarus_icons/*.png so each palette
    slot displays its component's icon.

  BUILD
  - build_win.bat: false-positive BUILD SUCCESS when bcc32 silently
    failed — the "if not exist %.obj" guard was satisfied by the
    previous build's stale .obj, so the link step used outdated code
    and reported success. Root-cause noted; users should delete
    source/hbbuilder_win.obj before building when edits don't seem to
    take effect.

2026-04-12 (Windows: font size round-trip, label auto-fit, project load fixes)

  FIXES
  - UI_GetProp("oFont") now converts LOGFONT.lfHeight (pixels) back to
    points before formatting, so regenerated code emits the original
    point size. Previously the point size drifted on every save (e.g.
    60pt saved → regenerated as "100" → reopened as 100pt → 167px).
  - Project loader: HB_ATokens(content, Chr(10)) left a trailing CR on
    each form name when the .hbp was stored with CRLF line endings.
    MemoRead("...\Form1\r.prg") silently returned "" and the form
    never loaded. Strip Chr(13) before AllTrim on each line.
  - CodeEditorClearTabs now sets bSettingText guard around SCI_SETTEXT
    so the live-sync debounced timer doesn't fire during project load
    (which was destroying the freshly-loaded form's children a few
    seconds after it appeared).
  - Inspector "Value" column now extends to the right edge of the
    inspector window (no 20-px margin).

  NEW
  - Labels auto-fit both height and width to the assigned font when
    oFont is applied: height derives from lfHeight + small leading;
    width uses GetTextExtentPoint32 on a memory DC (safe with no HWND,
    no shared screen-DC state) so it works both at load time and on
    live inspector edits.
  - TBRun's rebuild-skip hash now includes the backend C++ sources
    (hbbridge.cpp, tform.cpp, tcontrol.cpp, tcontrols.cpp), so changes
    to the IDE's runtime library force a rebuild of the user's
    UserApp.exe instead of running a stale cached binary.

2026-04-12 (Windows: Font dialog picks text color)

  Windows ChooseFont dialog now opens with CF_EFFECTS so the user can
  pick a text color in the same dialog (matching macOS, whose font
  panel embeds a color picker). oFont property now carries an optional
  third field "FaceName,Size,RRGGBB":
  - InsFontPick parses current value (face, size, optional hex color),
    seeds cf.rgbColors, and writes back a three-field string; it also
    pushes nClrText via UI_SetProp for immediate live feedback
  - hbbridge.cpp UI_SetProp("oFont") parses the optional color and
    stores it in FClrText; new "nClrText" property for direct access
  - TControl gains a COLORREF FClrText (CLR_INVALID = inherit)
  - TForm WM_CTLCOLORSTATIC/BTN/EDIT/LISTBOX applies SetTextColor when
    FClrText is set, independent of FClrPane
  - UI_GetProp("oFont") emits the third field only when FClrText is set

2026-04-12 (Windows: TLabel font preserved at runtime)

  FIX: Labels assigned an oFont in the designer now render with that
  font when the built project runs. Root cause: TForm::SetupChildren
  called SetFont(FFormFont) unconditionally before CreateHandle, which
  overwrote the per-control FFont set by ":oFont := " in the generated
  CreateForm() code (that runs before Activate(), when FHandle is 0).
  The two SetFont calls in tform.cpp (groupbox pass + generic pass) now
  skip controls that already have FFont, matching the macOS pattern
  ("if !FFont then inherit form font").

2026-04-12 (Windows: Live sync code editor → form designer + inspector)

  LIVE CODE-TO-DESIGNER SYNC (Windows):
  - Debounced text-change callback in Scintilla editor (500ms after last
    keystroke) — new pOnTextChange, debounceTimer (UINT_PTR), bSettingText
    fields in CODEEDITOR struct
  - WM_TIMER handler (id 7701) in CodeEdWndProc fires the Harbour block
    with (hEditor, nTab) after 500ms of inactivity via SetTimer/KillTimer
  - bSettingText guard in CodeEditorSetTabText and SwitchTab prevents the
    callback from firing when the IDE updates text programmatically
  - New HB_FUNC(CODEEDITORONTEXTCHANGE) to register callback from Harbour
  - OnEditorTextChange: clears form children, re-parses code via
    RestoreFormFromCode, refreshes inspector — only for form tabs
  - lSyncingFromCode static guard prevents SyncDesignerToCode from
    regenerating code while syncing from editor (bidirectional protection)
  - Cursor/scroll preservation: saves SCI_GETCURRENTPOS and
    SCI_GETFIRSTVISIBLELINE before callback, restores them after, clamps
    cursor to new document length
  - SCI_GETFIRSTVISIBLELINE (2152) and SCI_SETFIRSTVISIBLELINE (2613)
    defines added

2026-04-12 (Linux: Live sync code editor → form designer + inspector)

2026-04-09 (build_mac.sh: detect Scintilla architecture mismatch)

  BUILD FIX (macOS):
  - build_mac.sh now verifies cached libscintilla.a / liblexilla.a match
    the host architecture (arm64 vs x86_64) via 'lipo -archs' and rebuilds
    them automatically if mismatched
  - Previously the script only checked file existence, so stale libs from
    an Intel build or from a bad download would be silently reused on
    Apple Silicon, producing cryptic link errors:
       warning: ignoring file liblexilla.a(Accessor.o):
       found architecture 'x86_64', required architecture 'arm64'
       Undefined symbols: _CreateLexer, OBJC_CLASS$_ScintillaView
  - Reported by Marek Olszewski on macOS arm64

2026-04-09 (Cross-platform fix: classes.prg linker errors on macOS/Linux)

  BUILD FIX (macOS/Linux):
  - classes.prg had unconditional EXTERNAL UI_STORECLRPANE / UI_HASHANDLE
    declarations and a W32_ErrorDialog() call, all Windows-only symbols
    implemented in source/cpp/hbbridge.cpp. Because hbbuilder_macos.prg
    and hbbuilder_linux.prg both #include "classes.prg", the linker on
    macOS (and Linux) failed with undefined symbols:
       _HB_FUN_UI_HASHANDLE
       _HB_FUN_UI_STORECLRPANE
       _HB_FUN_W32_ERRORDIALOG
  - Wrapped both EXTERNAL declarations and the W32_ErrorDialog fallback
    call in #ifdef __PLATFORM__WINDOWS / #endif so they are only compiled
    into the Windows build
  - Reported by Marek Olszewski on macOS arm64 after pulling Session 33
    Windows fixes

2026-04-07 (Session 16: Win32 — ShowModal fix, project restore, inspector events)

  SHOWMODAL REWRITE (WIN32):
  - Replaced GetMessage+PostQuitMessage with PeekMessage+WaitMessage loop
    controlled by FModal flag. PostQuitMessage contaminated the main loop
    causing hangs after closing the modal form.
  - WM_CLOSE on modal forms now just clears FModal flag (no SW_HIDE, no
    DestroyWindow). ShowModal() handles cleanup in correct order:
    EnableWindow(owner) first, then DestroyWindow(modal).
  - Fixed visual distortion on modal close: removed forced RedrawWindow
    and unnecessary SetForegroundWindow. Windows auto-activates the owner
    since it was set as parent in CreateWindowExA.
  - Buttons with Default/Cancel now send WM_CLOSE instead of calling
    Close() directly, so the form's close handler runs correctly for
    modal, main, and secondary windows.

  PROJECT RESTORE (WIN32):
  - Added RestoreFormFromCode() — parses form .prg code to restore:
    Title, Width, Height, Left, Top, Color, and recreates all controls
    (Label, Button, Edit, CheckBox, ComboBox, GroupBox, ListBox,
    RadioButton, Memo) + non-visual components. Ported from Linux/GTK3.
  - TBOpen() now calls RestoreFormFromCode() for each form.
  - Only the first form is visible after loading; others are hidden
    with UI_FormHide() — matches Mac/Linux behavior.

  INSPECTOR EVENT FIX:
  - Fixed event handler name generation: InsPopulateEvents() indents
    event names with 6 spaces for display ("      OnClick"), but the
    double-click callback was passing those spaces to Harbour.
    Result: "Button1    OnClick" instead of "Button1Click".
    Now strips leading spaces before passing to the callback.

  BUILD FIXES:
  - Added UI_MSGBOX stub with MessageBoxA to user app build stubs
    (was missing after removing duplicate from hbbridge.cpp).
  - Added #include <windows.h> to user app stubs for MessageBoxA.
  - AllTrim() on control names in RegenerateFormCode/OnEventDblClick.

  SAVE DIALOG FIX:
  - Changed lpstrInitialDir from CSIDL_PERSONAL (OneDrive-redirected
    Documents) to CSIDL_DESKTOPDIRECTORY to avoid "file not found"
    error on OneDrive-enabled systems.
  - Removed OFN_PATHMUSTEXIST from Save dialog flags.
  - Removed debug trace code from TBSave().

  LAYOUT:
  - Splitter moved 90px left (nInsW reduced by 90px).

  SHOWMODAL (WIN32):
  - Implemented ShowModal() for TForm on Windows. Uses EnableWindow() to

    until form is closed, returns FModalResult (0/1/2).
  - Added FModal flag to distinguish modal forms from secondary (Show) windows.
  - WM_CLOSE/WM_DESTROY now handle three cases: FMainWindow (PostQuitMessage),
    FModal (PostQuitMessage exits nested loop), secondary (SW_HIDE only).
  - CreateWindowExA now passes hParent for proper owner chain.

    to reliably force windows to front on Windows.
  - CodeEditorBringToFront() uses same TOPMOST trick.
  - Added UI_FormIsKeyWindow(), UI_FormIsVisible(), UI_FormHide().

  FORM LIFECYCLE (WIN32):
  - Fixed MenuNewForm(): was calling Close() (DestroyWindow, FHandle=NULL)
    on the previous form. Changed to UI_FormHide() to preserve the handle.
    Now matches Mac/Linux behavior — forms can be re-shown when switching tabs.
  - Fixed SwitchToForm(): reordered to call CodeEditorSelectTab() before
    UI_FormBringToFront() so form stays on top. Added lSwitching guard to

2026-04-07 (Session 13: Form lifecycle, project restore & modal forms)

  MODAL FORMS:
  - Added ShowModal() method to TForm. Uses [NSApp runModalForWindow:]
    to block caller until the form is closed. Returns FModalResult
    (0=none, 1=default button, 2=cancel button).
  - windowWillClose: detects modal windows via [NSApp modalWindow] and
    calls [NSApp stopModal] instead of [NSApp stop:nil].
  - Usage: nResult := oForm2:ShowModal()

2026-04-07 (Session 13: Form lifecycle & project restore fixes)

  BUG FIXES:
  - Fixed crash when selecting File > New Form. MenuNewForm() was calling
    :Close() on the current design form, which triggers windowWillClose:
    → [NSApp stop:nil], killing the run loop. Changed to UI_FormHide()
    (orderOut:nil) which simply hides the window without stopping the app.
  - Added Hide() method to TForm class (INLINE UI_FormHide).
  - Fixed closing a secondary form (Form2) killing the entire app.
    Root cause: Activate() on Form2 created a nested [NSApp run] loop;
    closing it called [NSApp stop:nil] which collapsed both loops.
    Fix: prevent nested [NSApp run] via s_nRunLoopDepth counter;
    windowWillClose: only stops the loop if the form owned a modal loop
    (FRunning/FWasRunning guard).
  - Fixed project load not restoring form colors (nClrPane). The color
    was set via UI_SetProp before the NSWindow existed, so the visual
    update was skipped. Fix: apply FBgColor when creating the window,
    and pass it to the dot grid view at creation time.
  - Fixed project load not restoring form positions (::Left, ::Top).
    Added parsing of ::Left, ::Top, and ::Color in RestoreFormFromCode.

2026-04-07 (Session 12c: Debugger UX polish)

  DEBUGGER FIXES:
  - Fixed Scintilla marker message IDs: SCI_MARKERDELETEALL=2045 (was 2003),
    SCI_MARKERDELETE=2044 (was 2002). Old line markers now clear correctly.
  - Fixed crash on second Step: SCI_GOTOLINE via PostMessage (async) prevents
    re-entrant crash; SCI_COLOURISE and SetForegroundWindow removed from
    CodeEditorShowDebugLine.
  - Static buffers in dbghook.c prevent stack overflow in debug hook callback.
  - Client GO mode: DbgRecvNonBlock (hb_socketSelect timeout=0) allows
    DebugApp to run freely without blocking on every line. Client only sends
    PAUSE in stepping mode, not running mode.
  - IDE GO mode: message pump with disconnect detection (recv MSG_PEEK).
    User can click Step to return to stepping, or Stop to quit.

  DEBUGGER UX:
  - Inspector debug mode: INS_SetDebugMode switches to Vars/CallStack/Watch
    tabs, hides combo, title "Debugger". INS_SetDebugLocals parses VARS
    string with [PUBLIC]/[PRIVATE]/[LOCAL] categories. INS_SetDebugStack
    parses STACK string into CallStack tab (Function/Line columns).
  - On debug end: inspector restores Properties/Events, repopulates combo
    and properties from design form. Editor switches to form code tab.
  - Design form hidden during debug, restored on end.
  - Wait cursor: s_dbgWaitCursor flag forces IDC_WAIT in all message pumps
    (Accept, Recv) until first shouldPause=TRUE callback.
  - DebugApp window: HWND_TOPMOST/HWND_NOTOPMOST trick in TForm::Run()
    forces window to front. AllowSetForegroundWindow + BringDebugAppToFront
    with AttachThreadInput for Go mode.
  - DPI: SetProcessDPIAware removed from C++ static initializer (was
    affecting DebugApp), called from Harbour Main() only.
  - Platform stubs (UI_MEMONEW, MAC_RUNTIMEERRORDIALOG, MAC_APPTERMINATE)
    injected into both debug_main.prg and main.prg. iphlpapi.lib added
    to both MSVC and BCC link steps.

2026-04-07 (Session 12: Windows socket debugger + full dark mode)

  SOCKET DEBUGGER PORT TO WINDOWS (macOS/Linux parity):
  - Ported socket-based debugger from macOS/Linux to Windows
  - Winsock TCP server on port 19800 in hbbridge.cpp: DbgServerStart/Accept/
    Recv/Send/Stop using select() + PeekMessage for non-blocking I/O
  - IDE_DebugStart2: socket command loop with PAUSE/STEP/GO/QUIT protocol,
    CreateProcessA to launch DebugApp.exe, 30s accept timeout
  - TBDebugRun: assembles debug_main.prg (Project1 + forms + classes +
    dbgclient.prg + INIT PROCEDURE __DbgInit), compiles native exe with
    both MSVC and BCC support, links with hbdebug.lib + ws2_32.lib + iphlpapi.lib
  - CodeEditorShowDebugLine: Scintilla marker 11 (yellow bg) for current
    execution line, with scroll-to-line and editor bring-to-front
  - W32_DebugUpdateLocalsStr/StackStr: parse VARS/STACK strings from socket
    protocol into debug panel ListViews (categories, name=value(type) format)
  - OnDebugPause: 4-param callback (cFunc, nLine, cLocals, cStack) with line
    offset mapping (aDbgOffsets), framework auto-skip, DbgMapLocalNames for
    real variable names, DbgFixStackLines for editor tab coordinates
  - dbghook.c: static buffers to prevent stack overflow in debug hook callback,
    Windows _strnicmp compat (#define strncasecmp _strnicmp)
  - Platform stubs injected into debug_main.prg: UI_MEMONEW,
    MAC_RUNTIMEERRORDIALOG, MAC_APPTERMINATE (also in TBRun main.prg)
  - Removed legacy .hrb in-process debugger, removed W32_DebugPanel() call

  FULL DARK MODE (Windows 10/11):
  - IDE bar: dark background RGB(45,45,48) via UI_FormSetBgColor
  - Menu bar: dark via WM_NCPAINT/WM_NCACTIVATE painting over menu bar rect
    with GetWindowDC + GetMenuBarInfo, drawing items with DrawTextA
  - Menu popups: dark via SetPreferredAppMode(ForceDark) from uxtheme.dll
    ordinal 135, called in C++ static initializer before any window creation
  - Title bars: dark via DwmSetWindowAttribute(DWMWA_USE_IMMERSIVE_DARK_MODE)
    in TForm::Show() for all form windows, dynamic loading for BCC compat
  - AllowDarkModeForWindow (uxtheme ordinal 133) + RefreshImmersiveColorPolicyState
    (ordinal 104) for each window
  - Toolbars: text RGB(212,212,212) on RGB(45,45,48) via NM_CUSTOMDRAW
  - Inspector: dark background RGB(30,30,30), ListViews with dark alternating
    rows, category headers RGB(50,50,50), owner-draw tabs (TCS_OWNERDRAWFIXED),
    tab background subclass WM_ERASEBKGND, dark title bar, combo/edit dark
    via WM_CTLCOLOREDIT/WM_CTLCOLORLISTBOX/WM_CTLCOLORSTATIC
  - Code editor: owner-draw dark tabs, dark tab background subclass,
    dark title bar, dark status bar
  - Design form: dark background RGB(45,45,45), grid dots RGB(90,90,90),
    dark title bar via SetDarkTitleBar() dynamic loading
  - Component palette: owner-draw dark tabs (TCS_OWNERDRAWFIXED), dark
    tab background WM_ERASEBKGND, owner-draw icon buttons (BS_OWNERDRAW)
    with dark background + centered ImageList icons, dark splitter
  - View > Dark Mode toggle: saves DarkMode=1|0 to hbbuilder.ini,
    reads on startup, restart required to apply

  BUILD SYSTEM:
  - build_win.bat: auto-detects BCC, MSVC x86, MinGW compilers with
    user selection prompt when multiple found. Full build paths for all 3.
  - winsock2.h/winsock.h conflict resolved: _WINSOCKAPI_ define in
    hbbridge.cpp prevents windows.h from including winsock.h
  - dwmapi.h removed from tform.cpp (BCC doesn't have it), replaced
    with dynamic LoadLibrary("dwmapi.dll") + GetProcAddress

  GIT BACKEND (hbbridge.cpp, +11 HB_FUNC):

  GIT_Log() ............ parse `git log --format` → { {cHash, cAuthor, cDate, cMsg}, ... }

  GIT_CurrentBranch() .. get HEAD branch name
  GIT_Blame() .......... get blame output for a file

  GIT_RemoteList() ..... list remotes with URLs
  GIT_StashList() ...... list stash entries

  - Language/runtime interop: call Python, Swift, Go, Node, Rust,
    Java, .NET, Lua, Ruby from Harbour via their native C FFI APIs
  - Added to palette on all 3 platforms (Windows, Linux, macOS)

  WHY THESE LANGUAGES:
  - Python: #1 for AI/ML (TensorFlow, PyTorch), data science (pandas)
  - Swift: native macOS/iOS, required for Apple frameworks
  - Go: dominant in microservices, CLIs, cloud infrastructure
  - Node: npm ecosystem (2M+ packages), Electron, real-time
  - Rust: memory-safe systems code, WASM target, growing fast
  - Java: enterprise standard, Android, massive library ecosystem
  - DotNet: Windows enterprise (.NET/C#, WPF, Entity Framework)
  - Lua: ultra-lightweight (300KB), ideal for user scripting/plugins
  - Ruby: expressive DSLs, web (Rails), DevOps tooling

  PALETTE: 111 → 120 components, 14 → 15 tabs

  IDE_DebugGetLine() .... return current source line
  IDE_DebugGetModule() .. return current module name
  IDE_DebugGetLocals() .. inspect local variables (up to 30, with type)
  - State machine: IDLE → RUNNING/STEPPING/STEPOVER → PAUSED → STOPPED

2026-04-03 (Session 5b: Database Components + Data Controls)
--------------------------------------------------------------

DATABASE COMPONENTS (classes.prg - non-visual, Data Access tab):
  TDatabase ........... abstract base class with unified API:
                         Open/Close/Execute/Query/Tables/IsConnected/LastError
  TDBFTable ........... native DBF/NTX/CDX via Harbour RDD (20+ methods:
                         GoTop/Skip/Seek/Append/Delete/FieldGet/FieldPut/
                         RecNo/RecCount/Eof/Structure/CreateIndex)
  TSQLite ............. SQLite3 via hbsqlit3 (Execute/Query/CreateTable/
                         BeginTransaction/Commit/Rollback/LastInsertId)
  TMySQL .............. stub (needs libmysqlclient-dev)
  TMariaDB ........... inherits TMySQL (wire-compatible)
  TPostgreSQL ........ stub (needs libpq-dev)
  TFirebird .......... stub (needs firebird-dev)
  TSQLServer ......... stub (needs freetds-dev)
  TOracle ............ stub (needs Oracle Instant Client)
  TMongoDB ........... stub (needs libmongoc-dev)

  Architecture: all inherit TDatabase, same API. Changing backend = one line.

DATA CONTROLS (classes.prg - visual, Data Controls tab):
  TDataSource ........ binds TDatabase to visual controls
                        MoveFirst/Prev/Next/Last/Append/Delete/Save/Refresh
  TDBControl ......... base class (RefreshFromDB/WriteToDB)
  TDBText ............ label displaying field value
  TDBEdit ............ editable entry bound to field
  TDBComboBox ........ combo bound to field
  TDBCheckBox ........ check button bound to logical field
  TDBNavigator ....... 7 buttons (First/Prior/Next/Last/Insert/Remove/Post)

GTK3 WIDGETS (gtk3_core.c - Data Controls):
  HBDBGrid ........... GtkTreeView with 4 resizable columns + grid lines
  HBDBNavigator ...... GtkButtonBox with 7 navigation buttons
  HBDBText ........... GtkLabel bound to field
  HBDBEdit ........... GtkEntry bound to field
  HBDBComboBox ....... GtkComboBoxText bound to field
  HBDBCheckBox ....... GtkCheckButton bound to logical field
  HBDBImage .......... GtkFrame + GtkImage for blob/path fields

SAMPLE PROJECTS (samples/projects/database/):

2026-04-03 (Session 3: Scintilla Code Editor)
----------------------------------------------

MAJOR: Replaced RichEdit with Scintilla 5.6.1 + Lexilla 5.4.8

  Code editor completely rewritten to use Scintilla — the same editing
  component used by Notepad++, SciTE, Code::Blocks, and many professional IDEs.
  This replaces the RichEdit-based editor which had unreliable syntax coloring.

  SYNTAX HIGHLIGHTING (automatic via C/C++ lexer + Harbour keywords):
  - Keywords ......... bright blue, bold (function, local, if, return, class...)
  - Commands ......... teal/cyan (DEFINE, FORM, BUTTON, ACTIVATE...)
  - Comments ......... green, italic (// and /* */)
  - Strings .......... orange ("..." and '...')
  - Numbers .......... light green (123, 0xFF)
  - Preprocessor ..... magenta (#include, #define, #xcommand)
  - Operators ........ light gray
  - Default text ..... light gray on dark background (RGB 30,30,30)

  BUILT-IN FEATURES (no manual code needed):
  - Line numbers with dark gutter (replaced manual GutterPaint/double-buffer)
  - Code folding with box-style markers (click margin to fold/unfold)
  - Indentation guides (visual vertical lines)
  - UTF-8 support (SCI_SETCODEPAGE SC_CP_UTF8)
  - Auto-indent on Enter (preserves previous line indentation)
  - Native auto-complete popup (Ctrl+Space) with all Harbour keywords + functions

  KEYBOARD SHORTCUTS (all preserved from RichEdit version):
  - Ctrl+F ........... Find bar
  - Ctrl+H ........... Find & Replace bar
  - Ctrl+Space ....... Auto-complete
  - Ctrl+/ ........... Toggle line comment (//)
  - Ctrl+Shift+D ..... Duplicate line (SCI_LINEDUPLICATE)
  - Ctrl+Shift+K ..... Delete line (SCI_LINEDELETE)
  - Ctrl+L ........... Select entire line
  - Ctrl+G ........... Go to position
  - F3 / Shift+F3 .... Find Next / Previous
  - Esc .............. Close find bar

  FIND/REPLACE (rewritten for Scintilla API):
  - Uses SCI_SEARCHINTARGET instead of EM_FINDTEXT
  - Forward and backward search with wrap-around
  - Total match count displayed in status label

  REMOVED (~300 lines of manual code):
  - HighlightCode() .... manual token-by-token highlighting
  - SetRichColor() ..... EM_SETCHARFORMAT per range
  - GutterPaint() ...... manual line number painting with double-buffer
  - GutterSync() ....... gutter invalidation on scroll
  - GutterWndProc() .... separate gutter window class
  - CodeEditSubProc() .. RichEdit subclass for keyboard interception
  - IsKeyword() ........ manual keyword lookup
  - IsCommand() ........ manual command lookup
  - s_keywords[] ....... static keyword array (now in SCI_SETKEYWORDS)
  - s_commands[] ....... static command array (now in SCI_SETKEYWORDS)

  NEW FUNCTIONS:
  - InitScintilla() ........ loads Scintilla.dll + Lexilla.dll from resources/
  - ConfigureScintilla() ... sets lexer, keywords, colors, margins, folding

  FILES ADDED:
  - resources/Scintilla.dll .... Scintilla 5.6.1 (32-bit PE32, 824 KB)
  - resources/Lexilla.dll ...... Lexilla 5.4.8 (32-bit PE32, 1100 KB)
  - resources/scintilla/ ....... Full source code for all platforms
      scintilla_src/scintilla/win32/ ... Windows build files
      scintilla_src/scintilla/cocoa/ ... macOS framework + Xcode project
      scintilla_src/scintilla/gtk/ ..... Linux GTK3 build files
      lexilla_src/lexilla/ ............ Lexer library source
  - build_win.bat .............. Windows build script

  FIXED (BCC32 C-mode compatibility):
  - Non-const RECT initializers in W32_GeneratePaletteIcons
  - Non-const RECT initializers in W32_GenerateToolbarIcons
  - Declaration-after-statement in SCN_CHARADDED handler
  - Non-const array initializer in PO_HideAll

  TRACE LOGGING:
  - scintilla_trace.log: DLL loading, window creation, configuration

  PENDING:
  - macOS: compile ScintillaView framework, replace NSTextView in cocoa_core.m
  - Linux: compile libscintilla, replace GtkTextView in gtk3_core.c

2026-04-02 (HbBuilder: TForm properties, events, inspector tabs, code generation)
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
- Renamed IDE to "HbBuilder" (title bar, macOS app menu, executable name)

    OnActivate, OnDeactivate

  * Keyboard: OnKeyDown, OnKeyUp, OnKeyPress

  * OnCloseQuery returns .T./.F. to allow/prevent close

- Inspector: Properties/Events tab selector (NSSegmentedControl)
  * Events tab shows all events per control type grouped by category
  * Column headers change: Property/Value vs Event/Handler
- Inspector: double-click event generates METHOD handler (C++Builder pattern)
  * Handler name: ComponentName + EventWithoutOn (e.g. Button1Click)
  * Inserts METHOD declaration in CLASS block
  * Appends METHOD implementation with separator lines
  * If handler exists, jumps to it in code editor

  CodeEditorInsertAfter for IDE code generation support
- UI_GetAllEvents: returns event list per control type (TForm 19 events,
  TButton/TEdit/TCheckBox/TComboBox/TLabel/TGroupBox with appropriate events)
- Code generation follows C++Builder OOP pattern:
  * Project1.prg with TApplication that creates TForm1
  * Form1.prg with CLASS TForm1 FROM TForm (DATAs + METHODs)

2026-04-01 (Icon images fix)
----------------------------
- Fixed magenta transparency mask for BMP icon strips on macOS
  * Replaced NSBitmapImageRep colorAtX/setColor approach (fails on BMP
    without alpha channel) with direct CGBitmapContext RGBA pixel manipulation
  * Magenta pixels (R>240, G<16, B>240) correctly replaced with transparent
- Fixed Retina display icon count bug
  * NSImage size returns points (scaled by DPI), not pixels
  * Changed to CGImageGetWidth/Height for actual pixel dimensions
  * Fixes toolbar.bmp (288x32) being read as 192x21 → only 6 of 9 icons
- Fixed duplicate window creation when Show() called before Activate()
  * createWindowWithRunLoop now reuses existing NSWindow if already created
  * Re-creates children to pick up toolbar/palette added after Show()
- Toolbar icon images stored in FIconImages and applied at createViewInParent
  * Solves timing issue: UI_ToolBarLoadImages called before view exists
  * Icons auto-applied when toolbar view is actually created
- Extracted SliceBmpStrip() helper: shared by toolbar and palette image loading
  * Loads BMP strip, slices into 32xH tiles, applies magenta transparency
  * Eliminates code duplication between UI_ToolBarLoadImages/UI_PaletteLoadImages
- Toolbar buttons: 40x40 borderless with 28x28 icon images (Silk icon set)
- Palette buttons: 32x32 icons with magenta transparency
